an1.1:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 1
an1.1:0.2 1. Rpdivagga
an1.1:0.3 110
an1.1:1.0 1
an1.1:1.1 Eva me suta
an1.1:1.2 eka samaya bhagav svatthiya viharati jetavane anthapiikassa rme.
an1.1:1.3 Tatra kho bhagav bhikkh mantesi:
an1.1:1.4 bhikkhavoti.

an1.41:1.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, sliska v yavaska v micchpaihita hatthena v pdena v akkanta hattha v pda v bhecchati lohita v uppdessatti neta hna vijjati.
an1.41:1.2 Ta kissa hetu?
an1.41:1.3 Micchpaihitatt, bhikkhave, skassa.
an1.41:1.4 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, so vata bhikkhu micchpaihitena cittena avijja bhecchati, vijja uppdessati, nibbna sacchikarissatti neta hna vijjati.

an10.1:1.1 Eva me suta
an10.1:1.2 eka samaya bhagav svatthiya viharati jetavane anthapiikassa rme.
an10.1:1.3 Atha kho yasm nando yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.1:2.1 Kimatthiyni, bhante, kusalni slni kimnisasnti?
an10.1:2.2 Avippaisratthni kho, nanda, kusalni slni avippaisrnisasnti.
an10.1:3.1 Avippaisro pana, bhante, kimatthiyo kimnisasoti?
an10.1:3.2 Avippaisro kho, nanda, pmojjattho pmojjnisasoti.
an10.1:4.1 Pmojja pana, bhante, kimatthiya kimnisasanti?
an10.1:4.2 Pmojja kho, nanda, ptattha ptnisasanti.
an10.1:5.1 Pti pana, bhante, kimatthiy kimnisasti?
an10.1:5.2 Pti kho, nanda, passaddhatth passaddhnisasti.
an10.1:6.1 Passaddhi pana, bhante, kimatthiy kimnisasti?
an10.1:6.2 Passaddhi kho, nanda, sukhatth sukhnisasti.
an10.1:7.1 Sukha pana, bhante, kimatthiya kimnisasanti?
an10.1:7.2 Sukha kho, nanda, samdhattha samdhnisasanti.
an10.1:8.1 Samdhi pana, bhante, kimatthiyo kimnisasoti?
an10.1:8.2 Samdhi kho, nanda, yathbhtaadassanattho yathbhtaadassannisasoti.
an10.1:9.1 Yathbhtaadassana pana, bhante, kimatthiya kimnisasanti?
an10.1:9.2 Yathbhtaadassana kho, nanda, nibbidvirgattha nibbidvirgnisasanti.
an10.1:10.1 Nibbidvirgo pana, bhante, kimatthiyo kimnisasoti?
an10.1:10.2 Nibbidvirgo kho, nanda, vimuttiadassanattho vimuttiadassannisaso.
an10.1:11.1 Iti kho, nanda, kusalni slni avippaisratthni avippaisrnisasni;
an10.1:11.2 avippaisro pmojjattho pmojjnisaso;
an10.1:11.3 pmojja ptattha ptnisasa;
an10.1:11.4 pti passaddhatth passaddhnisas;
an10.1:11.5 passaddhi sukhatth sukhnisas;
an10.1:11.6 sukha samdhattha samdhnisasa;
an10.1:11.7 samdhi yathbhtaadassanattho yathbhtaadassannisaso;
an10.1:11.8 yathbhtaadassana nibbidvirgattha nibbidvirgnisasa;
an10.1:11.9 nibbidvirgo vimuttiadassanattho vimuttiadassannisaso.
an10.1:11.10 Iti kho, nanda, kusalni slni anupubbena aggya parentti.
an10.1:11.11 Pahama. "

an10.2:0.3 Cetankarayasutta
an10.2:1.1 Slavato, bhikkhave, slasampannassa na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.2 avippaisro me uppajjatti.
an10.2:1.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya slavato slasampannassa avippaisro uppajjati.
an10.2:1.4 Avippaisrissa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.5 pmojja me uppajjatti.
an10.2:1.6 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya avippaisrissa pmojja jyati.
an10.2:1.7 Pamuditassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.8 pti me uppajjatti.
an10.2:1.9 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya pamuditassa pti uppajjati.
an10.2:1.10 Ptimanassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.11 kyo me passambhatti.
an10.2:1.12 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya ptimanassa kyo passambhati.
an10.2:1.13 Passaddhakyassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.14 sukha vediymti.
an10.2:1.15 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya passaddhakyo sukha vediyati.
an10.2:1.16 Sukhino, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.17 citta me samdhiyatti.
an10.2:1.18 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya sukhino citta samdhiyati.
an10.2:1.19 Samhitassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.20 yathbhta jnmi passmti.
an10.2:1.21 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya samhito yathbhta jnti passati.
an10.2:1.22 Yathbhta, bhikkhave, jnato passato na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.23 nibbindmi virajjmti.
an10.2:1.24 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya yathbhta jna passa nibbindati virajjati.
an10.2:1.25 Nibbinnassa, bhikkhave, virattassa na cetanya karaya:
an10.2:1.26 vimuttiadassana sacchikaromti.
an10.2:1.27 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya nibbinno viratto vimuttiadassana sacchikaroti.
an10.2:2.1 Iti kho, bhikkhave, nibbidvirgo vimuttiadassanattho vimuttiadassannisaso;
an10.2:2.2 yathbhtaadassana nibbidvirgattha nibbidvirgnisasa;
an10.2:2.3 samdhi yathbhtaadassanattho yathbhtaadassannisaso;
an10.2:2.4 sukha samdhattha samdhnisasa;
an10.2:2.5 passaddhi sukhatth sukhnisas;
an10.2:2.6 pti passaddhatth passaddhnisas;
an10.2:2.7 pmojja ptattha ptnisasa;
an10.2:2.8 avippaisro pmojjattho pmojjnisaso;
an10.2:2.9 kusalni slni avippaisratthni avippaisrnisasni.
an10.2:2.10 Iti kho, bhikkhave, dhamm dhamme abhisandenti, dhamm dhamme pariprenti apr pra gamanyti.
an10.2:2.11 Dutiya. "

an10.3:0.3 Pahamaupanisasutta
an10.3:1.1 Dusslassa, bhikkhave, slavipannassa hatpaniso hoti avippaisro;
an10.3:1.2 avippaisre asati avippaisravipannassa hatpanisa hoti pmojja;
an10.3:1.3 pmojje asati pmojjavipannassa hatpanis hoti pti;
an10.3:1.4 ptiy asati ptivipannassa hatpanis hoti passaddhi;
an10.3:1.5 passaddhiy asati passaddhivipannassa hatpanisa hoti sukha;
an10.3:1.6 sukhe asati sukhavipannassa hatpaniso hoti sammsamdhi;
an10.3:1.7 sammsamdhimhi asati sammsamdhivipannassa hatpanisa hoti yathbhtaadassana;
an10.3:1.8 yathbhtaadassane asati yathbhtaadassanavipannassa hatpaniso hoti nibbidvirgo;
an10.3:1.9 nibbidvirge asati nibbidvirgavipannassa hatpanisa hoti vimuttiadassana.
an10.3:1.10 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, rukkho skhpalsavipanno. Tassa papaikpi na pripri gacchati, tacopi pheggupi sropi na pripri gacchati.
an10.3:1.11 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, dusslassa slavipannassa hatpaniso hoti avippaisro;
an10.3:1.12 avippaisre asati avippaisravipannassa hatpanisa hoti pe
an10.3:1.13 vimuttiadassana.
an10.3:2.1 Slavato, bhikkhave, slasampannassa upanisasampanno hoti avippaisro;
an10.3:2.2 avippaisre sati avippaisrasampannassa upanisasampanna hoti pmojja;
an10.3:2.3 pmojje sati pmojjasampannassa upanisasampann hoti pti;
an10.3:2.4 ptiy sati ptisampannassa upanisasampann hoti passaddhi;
an10.3:2.5 passaddhiy sati passaddhisampannassa upanisasampanna hoti sukha;
an10.3:2.6 sukhe sati sukhasampannassa upanisasampanno hoti sammsamdhi;
an10.3:2.7 sammsamdhimhi sati sammsamdhisampannassa upanisasampanna hoti yathbhtaadassana;
an10.3:2.8 yathbhtaadassane sati yathbhtaadassanasampannassa upanisasampanno hoti nibbidvirgo;
an10.3:2.9 nibbidvirge sati nibbidvirgasampannassa upanisasampanna hoti vimuttiadassana.
an10.3:2.10 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, rukkho skhpalsasampanno. Tassa papaikpi pripri gacchati, tacopi pheggupi sropi pripri gacchati.
an10.3:2.11 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, slavato slasampannassa upanisasampanno hoti avippaisro;
an10.3:2.12 avippaisre sati avippaisrasampannassa upanisasampanna hoti pe
an10.3:2.13 vimuttiadassananti.
an10.3:2.14 Tatiya. "

an10.6:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.6
an10.6:0.2 1. nisasavagga
an10.6:0.3 Samdhisutta
an10.6:1.1 Atha kho yasm nando yena bhagav tenupasakami pe ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.6:1.2 siy nu kho, bhante, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an10.6:1.3 Siy, nanda, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an10.6:2.1 Yath katha pana, bhante, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an10.6:3.1 Idhnanda, bhikkhu evasa hoti:
an10.6:3.2 eta santa eta pata yadida sabbasakhrasamatho sabbpadhipainissaggo tahkkhayo virgo nirodho nibbnanti.
an10.6:3.3 Eva kho, nanda, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an10.6:3.4 Chaha. "
an10.7:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.7
an10.7:0.2 1. nisasavagga
an10.7:0.3 Sriputtasutta
an10.7:1.1 Atha kho yasm nando yenyasm sriputto tenupasakami; upasakamitv yasmat sriputtena saddhi sammodi.
an10.7:1.2 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando yasmanta sriputta etadavoca:
an10.7:2.1 Siy nu kho, vuso sriputta, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an10.7:3.1 Siy, vuso nanda, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe na paraloke paralokasa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an10.7:4.1 Yath katha pana, vuso sriputta, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe sa ca pana assti?
an10.7:4.2 Ekamidha, vuso nanda, samaya idheva svatthiya viharmi andhavanasmi.
an10.7:4.3 Tatthha tathrpa samdhi sampajji yath neva pathaviya pathavisa ahosi, na pasmi posa ahosi, na tejasmi tejosa ahosi, na vyasmi vyosa ahosi, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa ahosi, na viacyatane viacyatanasa ahosi, na kicayatane kicayatanasa ahosi, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa ahosi, na idhaloke idhalokasa ahosi, na paraloke paralokasa ahosi; sa ca pana ahosinti.
an10.7:5.1 Kisa panyasm sriputto tasmi samaye ahosti?
an10.7:5.2 Bhavanirodho nibbna bhavanirodho nibbnanti kho me, vuso, ava sa uppajjati ava sa nirujjhati.
an10.7:5.3 Seyyathpi, vuso, sakalikaggissa jhyamnassa ava acci uppajjati ava acci nirujjhati;
an10.7:5.4 evameva kho, vuso, bhavanirodho nibbna bhavanirodho nibbnanti ava sa uppajjati ava sa nirujjhati.
an10.7:5.5 Bhavanirodho nibbnanti sa ca panha, vuso, tasmi samaye ahosinti.
an10.7:5.6 Sattama. "
an10.8:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.8
an10.8:0.2 1. nisasavagga
an10.8:0.3 Jhnasutta
an10.8:1.1 Saddho ca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu hoti, no ca slav;
an10.8:1.2 eva so tenagena aparipro hoti.
an10.8:1.3 Tena ta aga paripretabba:
an10.8:1.4 kintha saddho ca assa, slav cti.
an10.8:1.5 Yato ca kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu saddho ca hoti slav ca, eva so tenagena paripro hoti.
an10.8:2.1 Saddho ca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu hoti slav ca, no ca bahussuto pe
an10.8:2.2 bahussuto ca, no ca dhammakathiko
an10.8:2.3 dhammakathiko ca, no ca parisvacaro
an10.8:2.4 parisvacaro ca, no ca visrado parisya dhamma deseti
an10.8:2.5 visrado ca parisya dhamma deseti, no ca vinayadharo
an10.8:2.6 vinayadharo ca, no ca raiko pantasensano
an10.8:2.7 raiko ca pantasensano, no ca catunna jhnna bhicetasikna dihadhammasukhavihrna nikmalbh hoti akicchalbh akasiralbh
an10.8:2.8 catunnaca jhnna bhicetasikna dihadhammasukhavihrna nikmalbh hoti akicchalbh akasiralbh, no ca savna khay ansava cetovimutti pavimutti diheva dhamme saya abhi sacchikatv upasampajja viharati.
an10.8:2.9 Eva so tenagena aparipro hoti.
an10.8:2.10 Tena ta aga paripretabba:
an10.8:2.11 kintha saddho ca assa, slav ca, bahussuto ca, dhammakathiko ca, parisvacaro ca, visrado ca parisya dhamma deseyya, vinayadharo ca, raiko ca pantasensano, catunnaca jhnna bhicetasikna dihadhammasukhavihrna nikmalbh assa akicchalbh akasiralbh, savnaca khay ansava cetovimutti pavimutti diheva dhamme saya abhi sacchikatv upasampajja vihareyyanti.
an10.8:3.1 Yato ca kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu saddho ca hoti, slav ca, bahussuto ca, dhammakathiko ca, parisvacaro ca, visrado ca parisya dhamma deseti, vinayadharo ca, raiko ca pantasensano, catunnaca jhnna bhicetasikna dihadhammasukhavihrna nikmalbh hoti akicchalbh akasiralbh, savnaca khay ansava cetovimutti pavimutti diheva dhamme saya abhi sacchikatv upasampajja viharati;
an10.8:3.2 eva so tenagena paripro hoti.
an10.8:3.3 Imehi kho, bhikkhave, dasahi dhammehi samanngato bhikkhu samantapsdiko ca hoti sabbkraparipro cti.
an10.8:3.4 Ahama. "

an10.10:2.9 Eva so tenagena aparipro hoti.
an10.10:2.10 Tena ta aga paripretabba:
an10.10:2.11 kintha saddho ca assa, slav ca, bahussuto ca, dhammakathiko ca, parisvacaro ca, visrado ca parisya dhamma deseyya, vinayadharo ca, anekavihitaca pubbenivsa anussareyya, seyyathidaekampi jti dvepi jtiyo pe iti skra sauddesa anekavihita pubbenivsa anussareyya, dibbena ca cakkhun visuddhena atikkantamnusakena pe yathkammpage satte pajneyya, savnaca khay pe sacchikatv upasampajja vihareyyanti.
an10.10:3.1 Yato ca kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu saddho ca hoti, slav ca, bahussuto ca, dhammakathiko ca, parisvacaro ca, visrado ca parisya dhamma deseti, vinayadharo ca, anekavihitaca pubbenivsa anussarati, seyyathidaekampi jti dvepi jtiyo pe iti skra sauddesa anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati, dibbena ca cakkhun visuddhena atikkantamnusakena pe yathkammpage satte pajnti, savnaca khay ansava cetovimutti pavimutti diheva dhamme saya abhi sacchikatv upasampajja viharati.
an10.10:3.2 Eva so tenagena paripro hoti.
an10.10:3.3 Imehi kho, bhikkhave, dasahi dhammehi samanngato bhikkhu samantapsdiko ca hoti sabbkraparipro cti.
an10.10:3.4 Dasama.
an10.10:3.5 nisasavaggo pahamo.
an10.10:4.0 Tassuddna
an10.10:4.1 Kimatthiya cetan ca,
an10.10:4.2 tayo upanispi ca;
an10.10:4.3 Samdhi sriputto ca,
an10.10:4.4 jhna santena vijjayti. "
an10.11:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.11
an10.11:0.2 2. Nthavagga
an10.11:0.3 Sensanasutta
an10.11:1.1 Pacagasamanngato, bhikkhave, bhikkhu pacagasamanngata sensana sevamno bhajamno nacirasseva savna khay ansava cetovimutti pavimutti diheva dhamme saya abhi sacchikatv upasampajja vihareyya.
an10.11:2.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu pacagasamanngato hoti?
an10.11:2.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu saddho hoti; saddahati tathgatassa bodhi:
an10.11:2.3 itipi so bhagav pe bhagavti;
an10.11:2.4 appbdho hoti apptako, samavepkiniy gahaiy samanngato ntistya nccuhya majjhimya padhnakkhamya;
an10.11:2.5 asaho hoti amyv, yathbhta attna vikatt satthari v visu v sabrahmacrsu;
an10.11:2.6 raddhavriyo viharati, akusalna dhammna pahnya, kusalna dhammna upasampadya; thmav dahaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu;
an10.11:2.7 paav hoti, udayatthagminiy paya samanngato ariyya nibbedhikya samm dukkhakkhayagminiy.
an10.11:2.8 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu pacagasamanngato hoti.
an10.11:3.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, sensana pacagasamanngata hoti?
an10.11:3.2 Idha, bhikkhave, sensana ntidra hoti nccsanna gamangamanasampanna
an10.11:3.3 div appkia ratti appasadda appanigghosa
an10.11:3.4 appaasamakasavttapasarsapasamphassa;
an10.11:3.5 tasmi kho pana sensane viharantassa appakasirena uppajjanti cvarapiaptasensanagilnapaccayabhesajjaparikkhr;
an10.11:3.6 tasmi kho pana sensane ther bhikkh viharanti bahussut gatgam dhammadhar vinayadhar mtikdhar;
an10.11:3.7 te klena kla upasakamitv paripucchati paripahati:
an10.11:3.8 ida, bhante, katha, imassa ko atthoti;
an10.11:3.9 tassa te yasmanto avivaaceva vivaranti anuttnkataca uttni karonti anekavihitesu ca kakhhniyesu dhammesu kakha paivinodenti.
an10.11:3.10 Eva kho, bhikkhave, sensana pacagasamanngata hoti.
an10.11:3.11 Pacagasamanngato kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu pacagasamanngata sensana sevamno bhajamno nacirasseva savna khay pe sacchikatv upasampajja vihareyyti.
an10.11:3.12 Pahama. "

an10.14:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.14
an10.14:0.2 2. Nthavagga
an10.14:0.3 Cetokhilasutta
an10.14:1.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa v bhikkhuniy v paca cetokhil appahn paca cetasovinibandh asamucchinn, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati hniyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no vuddhi.
an10.14:2.1 Katamassa paca cetokhil appahn honti?
an10.14:2.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu satthari kakhati vicikicchati ndhimuccati na sampasdati.
an10.14:2.3 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu satthari kakhati vicikicchati ndhimuccati na sampasdati, tassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:2.4 Yassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pahamo cetokhilo appahno hoti.
an10.14:3.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dhamme kakhati pe
an10.14:3.2 saghe kakhati
an10.14:3.3 sikkhya kakhati
an10.14:3.4 sabrahmacrsu kupito hoti anattamano hatacitto khilajto.
an10.14:3.5 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabrahmacrsu kupito hoti anattamano hatacitto khilajto, tassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:3.6 Yassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pacamo cetokhilo appahno hoti.
an10.14:3.7 Imassa paca cetokhil appahn honti.
an10.14:4.1 Katamassa paca cetasovinibandh asamucchinn honti?
an10.14:4.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kmesu avtargo hoti avigatacchando avigatapemo avigatapipso avigatapariho avigatataho.
an10.14:4.3 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kmesu avtargo hoti avigatacchando avigatapemo avigatapipso avigatapariho avigatataho, tassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:4.4 Yassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pahamo cetasovinibandho asamucchinno hoti.
an10.14:5.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kye avtargo hoti pe
an10.14:5.2 rpe avtargo hoti pe
an10.14:5.3 yvadattha udarvadehaka bhujitv seyyasukha passasukha middhasukha anuyutto viharati
an10.14:5.4 aatara devanikya paidhya brahmacariya carati: iminha slena v vatena v tapena v brahmacariyena v devo v bhavissmi devaataro vti.
an10.14:5.5 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu aatara devanikya paidhya brahmacariya carati: iminha slena v vatena v tapena v brahmacariyena v devo v bhavissmi devaataro vti, tassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:5.6 Yassa citta na namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pacamo cetasovinibandho asamucchinno hoti.
an10.14:5.7 Imassa paca cetasovinibandh asamucchinn honti.
an10.14:6.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa v bhikkhuniy v ime paca cetokhil appahn ime paca cetasovinibandh asamucchinn, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati hniyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no vuddhi.
an10.14:7.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, kapakkhe candassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati, hyateva vaena hyati maalena hyati bhya hyati rohaparihena;
an10.14:7.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, yassa kassaci bhikkhussa v bhikkhuniy v ime paca cetokhil appahn ime paca cetasovinibandh asamucchinn, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati hniyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no vuddhi.
an10.14:8.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa v bhikkhuniy v paca cetokhil pahn paca cetasovinibandh susamucchinn, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati vuddhiyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no parihni.
an10.14:9.1 Katamassa paca cetokhil pahn honti?
an10.14:9.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu satthari na kakhati na vicikicchati, adhimuccati sampasdati.
an10.14:9.3 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu satthari na kakhati na vicikicchati adhimuccati sampasdati, tassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:9.4 Yassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pahamo cetokhilo pahno hoti.
an10.14:10.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dhamme na kakhati pe
an10.14:10.2 saghe na kakhati
an10.14:10.3 sikkhya na kakhati
an10.14:10.4 sabrahmacrsu na kupito hoti attamano na hatacitto na khilajto.
an10.14:10.5 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabrahmacrsu na kupito hoti attamano na hatacitto na khilajto, tassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:10.6 Yassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pacamo cetokhilo pahno hoti.
an10.14:10.7 Imassa paca cetokhil pahn honti.
an10.14:11.1 Katamassa paca cetasovinibandh susamucchinn honti?
an10.14:11.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kmesu vtargo hoti vigatacchando vigatapemo vigatapipso vigatapariho vigatataho.
an10.14:11.3 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kmesu vtargo hoti vigatacchando vigatapemo vigatapipso vigatapariho vigatataho, tassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:11.4 Yassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pahamo cetasovinibandho susamucchinno hoti.
an10.14:12.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kye vtargo hoti pe
an10.14:12.2 rpe vtargo hoti pe
an10.14:12.3 na yvadattha udarvadehaka bhujitv seyyasukha passasukha middhasukha anuyutto viharati,
an10.14:12.4 na aatara devanikya paidhya brahmacariya carati: iminha slena v vatena v tapena v brahmacariyena v devo v bhavissmi devaataro vti.
an10.14:12.5 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na aatara devanikya paidhya pe devaataro vti, tassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya.
an10.14:12.6 Yassa citta namati tappya anuyogya staccya padhnya, evamassya pacamo cetasovinibandho susamucchinno hoti.
an10.14:12.7 Imassa paca cetasovinibandh susamucchinn honti.
an10.14:13.1 Yassa kassaci, bhikkhave, bhikkhussa v bhikkhuniy v ime paca cetokhil pahn ime paca cetasovinibandh susamucchinn, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati vuddhiyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no parihni.
an10.14:14.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, juhapakkhe candassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati, vahateva vaena vahati maalena vahati bhya vahati rohaparihena;
an10.14:14.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, yassa kassaci bhikkhussa v bhikkhuniy v ime paca cetokhil pahn ime paca cetasovinibandh susamucchinn, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati vuddhiyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no parihnti.
an10.14:14.3 Catuttha. "

an10.15:0.3 Appamdasutta
an10.15:1.1 Yvat, bhikkhave, satt apad v dvipad v catuppad v bahuppad v rpino v arpino v saino v asaino v nevasainsaino v, tathgato tesa aggamakkhyati araha sammsambuddho;
an10.15:1.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, ye keci kusal dhamm, sabbe te appamdamlak appamdasamosara. Appamdo tesa aggamakkhyati.
an10.15:2.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, yni knici jagalna pna padajtni, sabbni tni hatthipade samodhna gacchanti, hatthipada tesa aggamakkhyati, yadida mahantattena;
an10.15:2.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, ye keci kusal dhamm, sabbe te appamdamlak appamdasamosara. Appamdo tesa aggamakkhyati.
an10.15:3.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, kgrassa y kci gopnasiyo sabb t kagam kaninn kasamosara, ko tsa aggamakkhyati;
an10.15:3.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, ye keci kusal dhamm, sabbe te appamdamlak appamdasamosara. Appamdo tesa aggamakkhyati.
an10.15:4.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, ye keci mlagandh, knusriya tesa aggamakkhyati;
an10.15:4.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave pe.
an10.15:5.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, ye keci sragandh, lohitacandana tesa aggamakkhyati;
an10.15:5.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave pe.
an10.15:6.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, ye keci pupphagandh, vassika tesa aggamakkhyati;
an10.15:6.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave pe.
an10.15:7.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, ye keci khuddarjno, sabbe te rao cakkavattissa anuyant bhavanti, rj tesa cakkavatt aggamakkhyati;
an10.15:7.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave pe.
an10.15:8.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, y kci trakarpna pabh, sabb t candappabhya kala ngghanti soasi, candappabh tsa aggamakkhyati;
an10.15:8.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave pe.
an10.15:9.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, saradasamaye viddhe vigatavalhake deve dicco nabha abbhussakkamno sabba ksagata tamagata abhivihacca bhsate ca tapate ca virocati ca;
an10.15:9.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave pe.
an10.15:10.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, y kci mahnadiyo, seyyathidagag, yamun, aciravat, sarabh, mah, sabb t samuddagam samuddaninn samuddapo samuddapabbhr, mahsamuddo tsa aggamakkhyati;
an10.15:10.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, ye keci kusal dhamm, sabbe te appamdamlak appamdasamosara. Appamdo tesa aggamakkhyatti.
an10.15:10.3 Pacama. "

an10.17:5.3 ayampi dhammo nthakarao.

an10.17:7.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu raddhavriyo viharati akusalna dhammna pahnya, kusalna dhammna upasampadya, thmav dahaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu,

an10.22:0.2 3. Mahvagga
an10.22:0.3 Adhivuttipadasutta
an10.22:1.1 Atha kho yasm nando yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinna kho yasmanta nanda bhagav etadavoca:
an10.22:2.1 Ye te, nanda, dhamm tesa tesa adhivuttipadna abhi sacchikiriyya savattanti, visrado aha, nanda, tattha paijnmi.
an10.22:2.2 Tesa tesa tath tath dhamma desetu yath yath paipanno santa v atthti assati, asanta v natthti assati, hna v hnanti assati, pata v patanti assati, sauttara v sauttaranti assati, anuttara v anuttaranti assati;
an10.22:2.3 yath yath v pana ta teyya v daheyya v sacchikareyya v tath tath assati v dakkhati v sacchikarissati vti hnameta vijjati.
an10.22:2.4 Etadnuttariya, nanda, na yadida tattha tattha yathbhtaa.
an10.22:2.5 Etasm cha, nanda, aa a uttaritara v patatara v natthti vadmi.
an10.22:3.1 Dasayimni, nanda, tathgatassa tathgatabalni, yehi balehi samanngato tathgato sabha hna paijnti, parissu shanda nadati, brahmacakka pavatteti.
an10.22:3.2 Katamni dasa?
an10.22:3.3 Idhnanda, tathgato hnaca hnato ahnaca ahnato yathbhta pajnti.
an10.22:3.4 Yampnanda, tathgato hnaca hnato ahnaca ahnato yathbhta pajnti, idampnanda, tathgatassa tathgatabala hoti, ya bala gamma tathgato sabha hna paijnti, parissu shanda nadati, brahmacakka pavatteti.
an10.22:4.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato attngatapaccuppannna kammasamdnna hnaso hetuso vipka yathbhta pajnti.
an10.22:4.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:5.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato sabbatthagmini paipada yathbhta pajnti.
an10.22:5.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:6.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato anekadhtu nndhtu loka yathbhta pajnti.
an10.22:6.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:7.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato sattna nndhimuttikata yathbhta pajnti.
an10.22:7.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:8.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato parasattna parapuggalna indriyaparopariyatta yathbhta pajnti.
an10.22:8.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:9.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato jhnavimokkhasamdhisampattna sakilesa vodna vuhna yathbhta pajnti.
an10.22:9.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:10.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati, seyyathidaekampi jti dvepi jtiyo pe iti skra sauddesa anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati.
an10.22:10.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:11.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato dibbena cakkhun visuddhena atikkantamnusakena pe yathkammpage satte pajnti.
an10.22:11.2 Yampnanda pe idampnanda pe.
an10.22:12.1 Puna capara, nanda, tathgato savna khay ansava cetovimutti pavimutti diheva dhamme saya abhi sacchikatv upasampajja viharati.
an10.22:12.2 Yampnanda, tathgato savna khay ansava cetovimutti pe sacchikatv upasampajja viharati. Idampnanda, tathgatassa tathgatabala hoti, ya bala gamma tathgato sabha hna paijnti, parissu shanda nadati, brahmacakka pavatteti.
an10.22:13.1 Imni kho, nanda, dasa tathgatassa tathgatabalni, yehi balehi samanngato tathgato sabha hna paijnti, parissu shanda nadati, brahmacakka pavattetti.
an10.22:13.2 Dutiya. "
an10.23:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.23
an10.23:0.2 3. Mahvagga
an10.23:0.3 Kyasutta
an10.23:1.1 Atthi, bhikkhave, dhamm kyena pahtabb, no vcya.
an10.23:1.2 Atthi, bhikkhave, dhamm vcya pahtabb, no kyena.
an10.23:1.3 Atthi, bhikkhave, dhamm neva kyena pahtabb no vcya, paya disv pahtabb.
an10.23:2.1 Katame ca, bhikkhave, dhamm kyena pahtabb, no vcya?
an10.23:2.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu akusala panno hoti kici desa kyena.
an10.23:2.3 Tamena anuvicca vi sabrahmacr evamhasu:
an10.23:2.4 yasm kho akusala panno kici desa kyena.
an10.23:2.5 Sdhu vatyasm kyaduccarita pahya kyasucarita bhvetti.
an10.23:2.6 So anuvicca vihi sabrahmacrhi vuccamno kyaduccarita pahya kyasucarita bhveti.
an10.23:2.7 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, dhamm kyena pahtabb, no vcya.
an10.23:3.1 Katame ca, bhikkhave, dhamm vcya pahtabb, no kyena?
an10.23:3.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu akusala panno hoti kici desa vcya.
an10.23:3.3 Tamena anuvicca vi sabrahmacr evamhasu:
an10.23:3.4 yasm kho akusala panno kici desa vcya.
an10.23:3.5 Sdhu vatyasm vacduccarita pahya vacsucarita bhvetti.
an10.23:3.6 So anuvicca vihi sabrahmacrhi vuccamno vacduccarita pahya vacsucarita bhveti.
an10.23:3.7 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, dhamm vcya pahtabb, no kyena.
an10.23:4.1 Katame ca, bhikkhave, dhamm neva kyena pahtabb no vcya, paya disv pahtabb?
an10.23:4.2 Lobho, bhikkhave, neva kyena pahtabbo no vcya, paya disv pahtabbo.

an10.23:4.8 paso

an10.23:5.1 Ppik, bhikkhave, iss neva kyena pahtabb no vcya, paya disv pahtabb.
an10.23:5.2 Katam ca, bhikkhave, ppik iss?
an10.23:5.3 Idha, bhikkhave, ijjhati gahapatissa v gahapatiputtassa v dhanena v dhaena v rajatena v jtarpena v.
an10.23:5.4 Tatratarassa dsassa v upavsassa v eva hoti:
an10.23:5.5 aho vatimassa gahapatissa v gahapatiputtassa v na ijjheyya dhanena v dhaena v rajatena v jtarpena vti.
an10.23:5.6 Samao v pana brhmao v lbh hoti cvarapiaptasensanagilnapaccayabhesajjaparikkhrna.
an10.23:5.7 Tatratarassa samaassa v brhmaassa v eva hoti:
an10.23:5.8 aho vata ayamyasm na lbh assa cvarapiaptasensanagilnapaccayabhesajjaparikkhrnanti.
an10.23:5.9 Aya vuccati, bhikkhave, ppik iss.
an10.23:6.1 Ppik, bhikkhave, icch neva kyena pahtabb no vcya, paya disv pahtabb.
an10.23:6.2 Katam ca, bhikkhave, ppik icch?
an10.23:6.3 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco assaddho samno saddhoti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.4 dusslo samno slavti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.5 appassuto samno bahussutoti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.6 sagaikrmo samno pavivittoti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.7 kusto samno raddhavriyoti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.8 muhassati samno upahitassatti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.9 asamhito samno samhitoti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.10 duppao samno paavti ma jneyyunti icchati;
an10.23:6.11 akhsavo samno khsavoti ma jneyyunti icchati.
an10.23:6.12 Aya vuccati, bhikkhave, ppik icch.
an10.23:6.13 Ime vuccanti, bhikkhave, dhamm neva kyena pahtabb no vcya, paya disv pahtabb.

an10.26:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.26
an10.26:0.2 3. Mahvagga
an10.26:0.3 Ksutta
an10.26:1.1 Eka samaya yasm mahkaccno avantsu viharati kuraraghare pavatte pabbate.
an10.26:1.2 Atha kho k upsik kuraragharik yenyasm mahkaccno tenupasakami; upasakamitv yasmanta mahkaccna abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinn kho k upsik kuraragharik yasmanta mahkaccna etadavoca:
an10.26:1.3 vuttamida, bhante, bhagavat kumripahesu:
an10.26:2.1 Atthassa patti hadayassa santi,
an10.26:2.2 Jetvna sena piyastarpa;
an10.26:2.3 Ekoha jhya sukhamanubodhi,
an10.26:2.4 Tasm janena na karomi sakkhi;
an10.26:2.5 Sakkh na sampajjati kenaci meti.
an10.26:3.1 Imassa kho, bhante, bhagavat sakhittena bhsitassa katha vitthrena attho dahabboti?
an10.26:4.1 Pathavkasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini, eke samaabrhma atthoti abhinibbattesu.
an10.26:4.2 Yvat kho, bhagini, pathavkasiasampattiparamat, tadabhisi bhagav.
an10.26:4.3 Tadabhiya bhagav assdamaddasa dnavamaddasa nissaraamaddasa maggmaggaadassanamaddasa.
an10.26:4.4 Tassa assdadassanahetu dnavadassanahetu nissaraadassanahetu maggmaggaadassanahetu atthassa patti hadayassa santi vidit hoti.
an10.26:5.1 pokasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini pe
an10.26:5.2 tejokasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini
an10.26:5.3 vyokasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini
an10.26:5.4 nlakasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini
an10.26:5.5 ptakasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini
an10.26:5.6 lohitakasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini
an10.26:5.7 odtakasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini
an10.26:5.8 ksakasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini
an10.26:5.9 viakasiasampattiparam kho, bhagini, eke samaabrhma atthoti abhinibbattesu.
an10.26:5.10 Yvat kho, bhagini, viakasiasampattiparamat, tadabhisi bhagav.
an10.26:5.11 Tadabhiya bhagav assdamaddasa dnavamaddasa nissaraamaddasa maggmaggaadassanamaddasa
an10.26:5.12 tassa assdadassanahetu dnavadassanahetu nissaraadassanahetu maggmaggaadassanahetu atthassa patti hadayassa santi vidit hoti.
an10.26:5.13 Iti kho, bhagini, ya ta vutta bhagavat kumripahesu:
an10.26:6.1 Atthassa patti hadayassa santi,
an10.26:6.2 Jetvna sena piyastarpa;
an10.26:6.3 Ekoha jhya sukhamanubodhi,
an10.26:6.4 Tasm janena na karomi sakkhi;
an10.26:6.5 Sakkh na sampajjati kenaci meti.
an10.26:7.1 Imassa kho, bhagini, bhagavat sakhittena bhsitassa eva vitthrena attho dahabboti.
an10.26:7.2 Chaha. "

an10.27:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav svatthiya viharati jetavane anthapiikassa rme.
an10.27:1.2 Atha kho sambahul bhikkh pubbahasamaya nivsetv pattacvaramdya svatthi piya pavisisu.
an10.27:1.3 Atha kho tesa bhikkhna etadahosi:
an10.27:1.4 atippago kho tva svatthiya piya caritu;
an10.27:1.5 yannna maya yena aatitthiyna paribbjakna rmo tenupasakameyymti.
an10.27:2.1 Atha kho te bhikkh yena aatitthiyna paribbjakna rmo tenupasakamisu; upasakamitv tehi aatitthiyehi paribbjakehi saddhi sammodisu.
an10.27:2.2 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdisu. Ekamanta nisinne kho te bhikkh te aatitthiy paribbjak etadavocu:
an10.27:3.1 Samao, vuso, gotamo svakna eva dhamma deseti:
an10.27:3.2 etha tumhe, bhikkhave, sabba dhamma abhijntha, sabba dhamma abhiya viharathti;
an10.27:3.3 mayampi kho, vuso, svakna eva dhamma desema:
an10.27:3.4 etha tumhe, vuso, sabba dhamma abhijntha, sabba dhamma abhiya viharathti.
an10.27:3.5 Idha no, vuso, ko viseso ko adhippayso ki nnkaraa samaassa v gotamassa amhka v, yadida dhammadesanya v dhammadesana anussaniy v anussaninti?
an10.27:4.1 Atha kho te bhikkh tesa aatitthiyna paribbjakna bhsita neva abhinandisu nappaikkosisu.
an10.27:4.2 Anabhinanditv appaikkositv uhysan pakkamisu:
an10.27:4.3 bhagavato santike etassa bhsitassa attha jnissmti.
an10.27:5.1 Atha kho te bhikkh svatthiya piya caritv pacchbhatta piaptapaikkant yena bhagav tenupasakamisu; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdisu. Ekamanta nisinn kho te bhikkh bhagavanta etadavocu:
an10.27:6.1 Idha maya, bhante, pubbahasamaya nivsetv pattacvaramdya svatthi piya pavisimh.
an10.27:6.2 Tesa no, bhante, amhka etadahosi:
an10.27:6.3 atippago kho tva svatthiya piya caritu;
an10.27:6.4 yannna maya yena aatitthiyna paribbjakna rmo tenupasakameyymti.
an10.27:6.5 Atha kho maya, bhante, yena aatitthiyna paribbjakna rmo tenupasakamimh; upasakamitv tehi aatitthiyehi paribbjakehi saddhi sammodimh.
an10.27:6.6 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdimh. Ekamanta nisinne kho, bhante, aatitthiy paribbjak amhe etadavocu:
an10.27:7.1 Samao, vuso, gotamo svakna eva dhamma deseti
an10.27:7.2 etha tumhe, bhikkhave, sabba dhamma abhijntha, sabba dhamma abhiya viharathti;
an10.27:7.3 mayampi kho, vuso, svakna eva dhamma desema
an10.27:7.4 etha tumhe, vuso, sabba dhamma abhijntha, sabba dhamma abhiya viharathti.

an10.27:8.2 Anabhinanditv appaikkositv uhysan pakkamimh:
an10.27:8.3 bhagavato santike etassa bhsitassa attha jnissmti.
an10.27:9.1 Evavdino, bhikkhave, aatitthiy paribbjak evamassu vacany:
an10.27:9.2 eko, vuso, paho eko uddeso eka veyykaraa, dve pah dve uddes dve veyykarani, tayo pah tayo uddes ti veyykarani, cattro pah cattro uddes cattri veyykarani, paca pah pacuddes paca veyykarani, cha pah cha uddes cha veyykarani, satta pah sattuddes satta veyykarani, aha pah ahuddes aha veyykarani, nava pah navuddes nava veyykarani, dasa pah dasuddes dasa veyykaranti.
an10.27:9.3 Eva puh, bhikkhave, aatitthiy paribbjak na ceva sampyissanti, uttari ca vighta pajjissanti.
an10.27:9.4 Ta kissa hetu?
an10.27:9.5 Yath ta, bhikkhave, avisayasmi.
an10.27:9.6 Nha ta, bhikkhave, passmi sadevake loke samrake sabrahmake sassamaabrhmaiy pajya sadevamanussya yo imesa pahna veyykaraena citta rdheyya, aatra tathgatena v tathgatasvakena v ito v pana sutv.

an10.27:10.2 iti kho paneta vutta. Kiceta paicca vutta?

an10.28:0.3 Dutiyamahpahsutta
an10.28:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav kajagalya viharati veuvane.
an10.28:1.2 Atha kho sambahul kajagalak upsak yena kajagalik bhikkhun tenupasakamisu; upasakamitv kajagalika bhikkhuni abhivdetv ekamanta nisdisu. Ekamanta nisinn kho kajagalak upsak kajagalika bhikkhuni etadavocu:
an10.28:2.1 Vuttamida, ayye, bhagavat mahpahesu:
an10.28:2.2 eko paho eko uddeso eka veyykaraa, dve pah dve uddes dve veyykarani, tayo pah tayo uddes ti veyykarani, cattro pah cattro uddes cattri veyykarani, paca pah pacuddes paca veyykarani, cha pah cha uddes cha veyykarani, satta pah sattuddes satta veyykarani, aha pah ahuddes aha veyykarani, nava pah navuddes nava veyykarani, dasa pah dasuddes dasa veyykaranti.
an10.28:2.3 Imassa nu kho, ayye, bhagavat sakhittena bhsitassa katha vitthrena attho dahabboti?

an10.28:3.2 api ca yath mettha khyati
an10.28:3.3 ta sutha, sdhuka manasi karotha, bhsissmti.
an10.28:3.4 Eva, ayyeti, kho kajagalak upsak kajagalikya bhikkhuniy paccassosu.

an10.28:10.1 Iti kho, vuso, ya ta vutta bhagavat sakhittena bhsitsu mahpahsu:
an10.28:10.2 eko paho eko uddeso eka veyykaraa pe
an10.28:10.3 dasa pah dasuddes dasa veyykaranti, imassa kho aha, vuso, bhagavat sakhittena bhsitassa eva vitthrena attha jnmi.
an10.28:10.4 kakhamn ca pana tumhe, vuso, bhagavantaeva upasakamitv etamattha paipuccheyytha.
an10.28:10.5 Yath vo bhagav bykaroti tath na dhreyythti.
an10.28:10.6 Eva, ayyeti kho kajagalak upsak kajagalikya kho bhikkhuniy bhsita abhinanditv anumoditv uhysan kajagalika bhikkhuni abhivdetv padakkhia katv yena bhagav tenupasakamisu; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdisu.
an10.28:10.7 Ekamanta nisinn kho kajagalak upsak yvatako ahosi kajagalikya bhikkhuniy saddhi kathsallpo, ta sabba bhagavato rocesu.
an10.28:11.1 Sdhu sdhu, gahapatayo.
an10.28:11.2 Pait, gahapatayo, kajagalik bhikkhun. Mahpa, gahapatayo, kajagalik bhikkhun.
an10.28:11.3 Macepi tumhe, gahapatayo, upasakamitv etamattha paipuccheyytha, ahampi ceta evameva bykareyya yath ta kajagalikya bhikkhuniy bykata.
an10.28:11.4 Eso ceva tassa attho. Evaca na dhreyythti.
an10.28:11.5 Ahama. "

an10.31:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.31
an10.31:0.2 4. Uplivagga
an10.31:0.3 Uplisutta
an10.31:1.1 Atha kho yasm upli yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm upli bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.31:1.2 kati nu kho, bhante, atthavase paicca tathgatena svakna sikkhpada paatta, ptimokkha uddihanti?
an10.31:2.1 Dasa kho, upli, atthavase paicca tathgatena svakna sikkhpada paatta, ptimokkha uddiha.
an10.31:2.2 Katame dasa?
an10.31:2.3 Saghasuhutya, saghaphsutya, dummakna puggalna niggahya, pesalna bhikkhna phsuvihrya, dihadhammikna savna savarya, samparyikna savna paightya, appasannna pasdya, pasannna bhiyyobhvya, saddhammahitiy, vinaynuggahya
an10.31:2.4 ime kho, upli, dasa atthavase paicca tathgatena svakna sikkhpada paatta, ptimokkha uddihanti.

an10.44:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav kusinrya viharati baliharae vanasae.

an10.44:1.4 Bhadanteti te bhikkh bhagavato paccassosu.
an10.44:1.5 Bhagav etadavoca:
an10.44:2.1 Codakena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun para codetukmena paca dhamme ajjhatta paccavekkhitv paca dhamme ajjhatta upahpetv paro codetabbo.
an10.44:2.2 Katame paca dhamm ajjhatta paccavekkhitabb?
an10.44:2.3 Codakena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun para codetukmena eva paccavekkhitabba:
an10.44:2.4 parisuddhakyasamcro nu khomhi, parisuddhenamhi kyasamcrena samanngato acchiddena appaimasena.
an10.44:2.5 Savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu noti?

an10.44:2.7 igha tva yasm kyika sikkhassti, itissa bhavanti vattro.
an10.44:3.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, codakena bhikkhun para codetukmena eva paccavekkhitabba:
an10.44:3.2 parisuddhavacsamcro nu khomhi, parisuddhenamhi vacsamcrena samanngato acchiddena appaimasena.

an10.44:3.4 No ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhu parisuddhavacsamcro hoti parisuddhena vacsamcrena samanngato acchiddena appaimasena, tassa bhavanti vattro:
an10.44:3.5 igha tva yasm vcasika sikkhassti, itissa bhavanti vattro.
an10.44:4.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, codakena bhikkhun para codetukmena eva paccavekkhitabba:
an10.44:4.2 metta nu kho me citta paccupahita sabrahmacrsu anghta.
an10.44:4.3 Savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu noti?

an10.44:4.5 igha tva yasm sabrahmacrsu metta citta upahpehti, itissa bhavanti vattro.
an10.44:5.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, codakena bhikkhun para codetukmena eva paccavekkhitabba:
an10.44:5.2 bahussuto nu khomhi sutadharo sutasannicayo, ye te dhamm dikaly majjhekaly pariyosnakaly sttha sabyajana kevalaparipua parisuddha brahmacariya abhivadanti, tathrp me dhamm bahussut honti dht vacas paricit manasnupekkhit dihiy suppaividdh.
an10.44:5.3 Savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu noti?
an10.44:5.4 No ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhu bahussuto hoti sutadharo sutasannicayo, ye te dhamm dikaly majjhekaly pariyosnakaly sttha sabyajana kevalaparipua parisuddha brahmacariya abhivadanti, tathrpssa dhamm bahussut honti dht vacas paricit manasnupekkhit dihiy suppaividdh, tassa bhavanti vattro:
an10.44:5.5 igha tva yasm gama pariypuassti, itissa bhavanti vattro.
an10.44:6.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, codakena bhikkhun para codetukmena eva paccavekkhitabba:
an10.44:6.2 ubhayni kho pana me ptimokkhni vitthrena svgatni honti suvibhattni suppavattni suvinicchitni suttaso anubyajanaso.

an10.44:6.4 No ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno ubhayni ptimokkhni vitthrena svgatni honti suvibhattni suppavattni suvinicchitni suttaso anubyajanaso, ida panyasm, kattha vutta bhagavatti, iti puho na sampyissati.
an10.44:6.5 Tassa bhavanti vattro:
an10.44:6.6 igha tva yasm vinaya sikkhassti, itissa bhavanti vattro.

an10.44:7.1 Katame paca dhamm ajjhatta upahpetabb?
an10.44:7.2 Klena vakkhmi, no aklena;

an10.44:7.7 ime paca dhamm ajjhatta upahpetabb.
an10.44:7.8 Codakena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun para codetukmena ime paca dhamme ajjhatta paccavekkhitv ime paca dhamme ajjhatta upahpetv paro codetabboti.

an10.47:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav vesliya viharati mahvane kgraslya.

an10.47:1.9 Aya kho, mahli, hetu, aya paccayo ppassa kammassa kiriyya ppassa kammassa pavattiyti.

an10.47:2.3 Adoso kho, mahli, hetu, adoso paccayo kalyassa kammassa kiriyya kalyassa kammassa pavattiy.
an10.47:2.4 Amoho kho, mahli, hetu, amoho paccayo kalyassa kammassa kiriyya kalyassa kammassa pavattiy.
an10.47:2.5 Yoniso manasikro kho, mahli, hetu, yoniso manasikro paccayo kalyassa kammassa kiriyya kalyassa kammassa pavattiy.
an10.47:2.6 Sammpaihita kho, mahli, citta hetu, sammpaihita citta paccayo kalyassa kammassa kiriyya kalyassa kammassa pavattiy.
an10.47:2.7 Aya kho, mahli, hetu, aya paccayo kalyassa kammassa kiriyya kalyassa kammassa pavattiy.
an10.47:2.8 Ime ca, mahli, dasa dhamm loke na savijjeyyu, nayidha payetha adhammacariyvisamacariyti v dhammacariysamacariyti v.

an10.51:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav svatthiya viharati jetavane anthapiikassa rme.

an10.51:3.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sacittapariyyakusalo hoti?
an10.51:3.2 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, itth v puriso v daharo yuv maanakajtiko dse v parisuddhe pariyodte acche v udakapatte saka mukhanimitta paccavekkhamno sace tattha passati raja v agaa v, tasseva rajassa v agaassa v pahnya vyamati.
an10.51:3.3 No ce tattha passati raja v agaa v, tenevattamano hoti paripuasakappo:
an10.51:3.4 lbh vata me, parisuddha vata meti.
an10.51:3.5 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno paccavekkha bahukr hoti kusalesu dhammesu:
an10.51:3.6 abhijjhlu nu kho bahula viharmi, anabhijjhlu nu kho bahula viharmi, bypannacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, abypannacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, thinamiddhapariyuhito nu kho bahula viharmi, vigatathinamiddho nu kho bahula viharmi, uddhato nu kho bahula viharmi, anuddhato nu kho bahula viharmi, vicikiccho nu kho bahula viharmi, tiavicikiccho nu kho bahula viharmi, kodhano nu kho bahula viharmi, akkodhano nu kho bahula viharmi, sakilihacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, asakilihacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, sraddhakyo nu kho bahula viharmi, asraddhakyo nu kho bahula viharmi, kusto nu kho bahula viharmi, raddhavriyo nu kho bahula viharmi, asamhito nu kho bahula viharmi, samhito nu kho bahula viharmti.
an10.51:4.1 Sace, bhikkhave, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno eva jnti:
an10.51:4.2 abhijjhlu bahula viharmi, bypannacitto bahula viharmi, thinamiddhapariyuhito bahula viharmi, uddhato bahula viharmi, vicikiccho bahula viharmi, kodhano bahula viharmi, sakilihacitto bahula viharmi, sraddhakyo bahula viharmi, kusto bahula viharmi, asamhito bahula viharmti, tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun tesayeva ppakna akusalna dhammna pahnya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.51:4.3 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, dittacelo v dittasso v. Tasseva celassa v ssassa v nibbpanya adhimatta chandaca vymaca usshaca ussohica appaivnica satica sampajaaca kareyya.
an10.51:4.4 Evameva kho tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun tesayeva ppakna akusalna dhammna pahnya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.51:5.1 Sace pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno eva jnti:
an10.51:5.2 anabhijjhlu bahula viharmi, abypannacitto bahula viharmi, vigatathinamiddho bahula viharmi, anuddhato bahula viharmi, tiavicikiccho bahula viharmi, akkodhano bahula viharmi, asakilihacitto bahula viharmi, asraddhakyo bahula viharmi, raddhavriyo bahula viharmi, samhito bahula viharmti, tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun tesuyeva kusalesu dhammesu patihya uttari savna khayya yogo karayoti.
an10.51:5.3 Pahama. "

an10.52:1.3 vusoti kho te bhikkh yasmato sriputtassa paccassosu.

an10.52:2.1 No ce, vuso, bhikkhu paracittapariyyakusalo hoti, atha sacittapariyyakusalo bhavissmti
an10.52:2.2 evahi vo, vuso, sikkhitabba.
an10.52:3.1 Kathacvuso, bhikkhu sacittapariyyakusalo hoti?
an10.52:3.2 Seyyathpi, vuso, itth v puriso v daharo yuv maanakajtiko dse v parisuddhe pariyodte acche v udapatte saka mukhanimitta paccavekkhamno sace tattha passati raja v agaa v, tasseva rajassa v agaassa v pahnya vyamati.
an10.52:3.3 No ce tattha passati raja v agaa v, tenevattamano hoti paripuasakappo:
an10.52:3.4 lbh vata me, parisuddha vata meti.
an10.52:4.1 Evameva kho, vuso, bhikkhuno paccavekkha bahukr hoti kusalesu dhammesu:
an10.52:4.2 abhijjhlu nu kho bahula viharmi, anabhijjhlu nu kho bahula viharmi, bypannacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, abypannacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, thinamiddhapariyuhito nu kho bahula viharmi, vigatathinamiddho nu kho bahula viharmi, uddhato nu kho bahula viharmi, anuddhato nu kho bahula viharmi, vicikiccho nu kho bahula viharmi, tiavicikiccho nu kho bahula viharmi, kodhano nu kho bahula viharmi, akkodhano nu kho bahula viharmi, sakilihacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, asakilihacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, sraddhakyo nu kho bahula viharmi, asraddhakyo nu kho bahula viharmi, kusto nu kho bahula viharmi, raddhavriyo nu kho bahula viharmi, samhito nu kho bahula viharmi, asamhito nu kho bahula viharmti.

an10.52:6.3 Dutiya. "

an10.53:1.1 hitimpha, bhikkhave, na vaaymi kusalesu dhammesu, pageva parihni.
an10.53:1.2 Vuhica kho aha, bhikkhave, vaaymi kusalesu dhammesu, no hiti no hni.
an10.53:2.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, hni hoti kusalesu dhammesu, no hiti no vuhi?
an10.53:2.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu yattako hoti saddhya slena sutena cgena paya paibhnena, tassa te dhamm neva tihanti no vahanti.
an10.53:2.3 Hnimeta, bhikkhave, vadmi kusalesu dhammesu, no hiti no vuhi.
an10.53:2.4 Eva kho, bhikkhave, hni hoti kusalesu dhammesu, no hiti no vuhi.

an10.53:3.3 hitimeta, bhikkhave, vadmi kusalesu dhammesu, no hni no vuhi.

an10.54:1.1 No ce, bhikkhave, bhikkhu paracittapariyyakusalo hoti, atha sacittapariyyakusalo bhavissmti
an10.54:1.2 evahi vo, bhikkhave, sikkhitabba.
an10.54:2.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sacittapariyyakusalo hoti?
an10.54:2.2 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, itth v puriso v daharo yuv maanakajtiko dse v parisuddhe pariyodte acche v udapatte saka mukhanimitta paccavekkhamno sace tattha passati raja v agaa v, tasseva rajassa v agaassa v pahnya vyamati.
an10.54:2.3 No ce tattha passati raja v agaa v, tenevattamano hoti paripuasakappo:
an10.54:2.4 lbh vata me, parisuddha vata meti.
an10.54:2.5 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno paccavekkha bahukr hoti kusalesu dhammesu:
an10.54:2.6 lbh nu khomhi ajjhatta cetosamathassa, na nu khomhi lbh ajjhatta cetosamathassa, lbh nu khomhi adhipadhammavipassanya, na nu khomhi lbh adhipadhammavipassanyti.
an10.54:3.1 Sace, bhikkhave, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno eva jnti:
an10.54:3.2 lbhmhi ajjhatta cetosamathassa, na lbh adhipadhammavipassanyti, tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun ajjhatta cetosamathe patihya adhipadhammavipassanya yogo karayo.
an10.54:3.3 So aparena samayena lbh ceva hoti ajjhatta cetosamathassa lbh ca adhipadhammavipassanya.
an10.54:4.1 Sace pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno eva jnti:
an10.54:4.2 lbhmhi adhipadhammavipassanya, na lbh ajjhatta cetosamathassti, tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun adhipadhammavipassanya patihya ajjhatta cetosamathe yogo karayo.
an10.54:4.3 So aparena samayena lbh ceva hoti adhipadhammavipassanya lbh ca ajjhatta cetosamathassa.
an10.54:5.1 Sace pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno eva jnti:
an10.54:5.2 na lbh ajjhatta cetosamathassa, na lbh adhipadhammavipassanyti, tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun tesayeva kusalna dhammna pailbhya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.54:5.3 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, dittacelo v dittasso v.
an10.54:5.4 Tasseva celassa v ssassa v nibbpanya adhimatta chandaca vymaca usshaca ussohica appaivnica satica sampajaaca kareyya.
an10.54:5.5 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, tena bhikkhun tesayeva kusalna dhammna pailbhya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.54:5.6 So aparena samayena lbh ceva hoti ajjhatta cetosamathassa lbh ca adhipadhammavipassanya.

an10.54:6.2 lbhmhi ajjhatta cetosamathassa, lbh adhipadhammavipassanyti, tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhun tesuyeva kusalesu dhammesu patihya uttari savna khayya yogo karayo.

an10.55:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.55
an10.55:0.2 6. Sacittavagga
an10.55:0.3 Parihnasutta
an10.55:1.1 Tatra kho yasm sriputto bhikkh mantesi:
an10.55:1.2 vuso bhikkhaveti.
an10.55:1.3 vusoti kho te bhikkh yasmato sriputtassa paccassosu.
an10.55:1.4 yasm sriputto etadavoca:
an10.55:2.1 Parihnadhammo puggalo, parihnadhammo puggaloti, vuso, vuccati.
an10.55:2.2 Aparihnadhammo puggalo, aparihnadhammo puggaloti, vuso, vuccati.
an10.55:2.3 Kittvat nu kho, vuso, parihnadhammo puggalo vutto bhagavat, kittvat ca pana aparihnadhammo puggalo vutto bhagavatti?
an10.55:2.4 Dratopi kho maya, vuso, gacchma yasmato sriputtassa santike etassa bhsitassa atthamatu.
an10.55:2.5 Sdhu vatyasmantayeva sriputta paibhtu etassa bhsitassa attho.
an10.55:2.6 yasmato sriputtassa sutv bhikkh dhressantti.
an10.55:3.1 Tenahvuso, sutha, sdhuka manasi karotha, bhsissmti.
an10.55:3.2 Evamvusoti kho te bhikkh yasmato sriputtassa paccassosu.
an10.55:3.3 yasm sriputto etadavoca:
an10.55:4.1 Kittvat nu kho, vuso, parihnadhammo puggalo vutto bhagavat?
an10.55:4.2 Idhvuso, bhikkhu assutaceva dhamma na suti, sut cassa dhamm sammosa gacchanti, ye cassa dhamm pubbe cetaso asamphuhapubb te cassa na samudcaranti, avitaceva na vijnti.
an10.55:4.3 Ettvat kho, vuso, parihnadhammo puggalo vutto bhagavat.
an10.55:5.1 Kittvat ca panvuso, aparihnadhammo puggalo vutto bhagavat?
an10.55:5.2 Idhvuso, bhikkhu assutaceva dhamma suti, sut cassa dhamm na sammosa gacchanti, ye cassa dhamm pubbe cetaso asamphuhapubb te cassa samudcaranti, avitaceva vijnti.
an10.55:5.3 Ettvat kho, vuso, aparihnadhammo puggalo vutto bhagavat.
an10.55:6.1 No ce, vuso, bhikkhu paracittapariyyakusalo hoti, atha sacittapariyyakusalo bhavissmti
an10.55:6.2 evahi vo, vuso, sikkhitabba.
an10.55:7.1 Kathacvuso, bhikkhu sacittapariyyakusalo hoti?
an10.55:7.2 Seyyathpi, vuso, itth v puriso v daharo yuv maanakajtiko dse v parisuddhe pariyodte acche v udapatte saka mukhanimitta paccavekkhamno sace tattha passati raja v agaa v, tasseva rajassa v agaassa v pahnya vyamati.
an10.55:7.3 No ce tattha passati raja v agaa v, tenevattamano hoti paripuasakappo:
an10.55:7.4 lbh vata me, parisuddha vata meti.
an10.55:7.5 Evameva kho, vuso, bhikkhuno paccavekkha bahukr hoti kusalesu dhammesu:
an10.55:7.6 anabhijjhlu nu kho bahula viharmi, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, abypannacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, vigatathinamiddho nu kho bahula viharmi, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, anuddhato nu kho bahula viharmi, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, tiavicikiccho nu kho bahula viharmi, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, akkodhano nu kho bahula viharmi, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, asakilihacitto nu kho bahula viharmi, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, lbh nu khomhi ajjhatta dhammapmojjassa, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, lbh nu khomhi ajjhatta cetosamathassa, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu no, lbh nu khomhi adhipadhammavipassanya, savijjati nu kho me eso dhammo udhu noti.
an10.55:8.1 Sace pana, vuso, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno sabbepime kusale dhamme attani na samanupassati, tenvuso, bhikkhun sabbesayeva imesa kusalna dhammna pailbhya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.55:8.2 Seyyathpi, vuso, dittacelo v dittasso v.
an10.55:8.3 Tasseva celassa v ssassa v nibbpanya adhimatta chandaca vymaca usshaca ussohica appaivnica satica sampajaaca kareyya.
an10.55:8.4 Evameva kho, vuso, tena bhikkhun sabbesayeva kusalna dhammna pailbhya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.55:9.1 Sace panvuso, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno ekacce kusale dhamme attani samanupassati, ekacce kusale dhamme attani na samanupassati, tenvuso, bhikkhun ye kusale dhamme attani samanupassati tesu kusalesu dhammesu patihya, ye kusale dhamme attani na samanupassati tesa kusalna dhammna pailbhya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.55:9.2 Seyyathpi, vuso, dittacelo v dittasso v.
an10.55:9.3 Tasseva celassa v ssassa v nibbpanya adhimatta chandaca vymaca usshaca ussohica appaivnica satica sampajaaca kareyya.
an10.55:9.4 Evameva kho, vuso, tena bhikkhun ye kusale dhamme attani samanupassati tesu kusalesu dhammesu patihya, ye kusale dhamme attani na samanupassati tesa kusalna dhammna pailbhya adhimatto chando ca vymo ca ussho ca ussoh ca appaivn ca sati ca sampajaaca karaya.
an10.55:10.1 Sace panvuso, bhikkhu paccavekkhamno sabbepime kusale dhamme attani samanupassati, tenvuso, bhikkhun sabbesveva imesu kusalesu dhammesu patihya uttari savna khayya yogo karayoti.
an10.55:10.2 Pacama. "

an10.61:6.23 Ko chro saddhya?
an10.61:6.24 Saddhammassavanantissa vacanya.
an10.61:6.25 Saddhammassavanampha, bhikkhave, shra vadmi, no anhra.
an10.61:6.26 Ko chro saddhammassavanassa?
an10.61:6.27 Sappurisasasevotissa vacanya.
an10.61:7.1 Iti kho, bhikkhave, sappurisasasevo paripro saddhammassavana paripreti, saddhammassavana paripra saddha paripreti, saddh paripr yonisomanasikra paripreti, yonisomanasikro paripro satisampajaa paripreti, satisampajaa paripra indriyasavara paripreti, indriyasavaro paripro ti sucaritni paripreti, ti sucaritni pariprni cattro satipahne pariprenti, cattro satipahn paripr satta bojjhage pariprenti, satta bojjhag paripr vijjvimutti pariprenti;
an10.61:7.2 evametiss vijjvimuttiy hro hoti, evaca pripri.
an10.61:8.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, uparipabbate thullaphusitake deve vassante ta udaka yathninna pavattamna pabbatakandarapadaraskh paripreti, pabbatakandarapadaraskh paripr kusobbhe pariprenti, kusobbh paripr mahsobbhe pariprenti, mahsobbh paripr kunnadiyo pariprenti, kunnadiyo paripr mahnadiyo pariprenti, mahnadiyo paripr mahsamudda sgara pariprenti;

an10.63:1.1 Ye keci, bhikkhave, mayi niha gat sabbe te dihisampann.
an10.63:1.2 Tesa dihisampannna pacanna idha nih, pacanna idha vihya nih.
an10.63:1.3 Katamesa pacanna idha nih?
an10.63:1.4 Sattakkhattuparamassa, kolakolassa, ekabjissa, sakadgmissa, yo ca diheva dhamme arah
an10.63:1.5 imesa pacanna idha nih.
an10.63:1.6 Katamesa pacanna idha vihya nih?
an10.63:1.7 Antarparinibbyissa, upahaccaparinibbyissa, asakhraparinibbyissa, sasakhraparinibbyissa, uddhasotassa akanihagmino
an10.63:1.8 imesa pacanna idha vihya nih.
an10.63:1.9 Ye keci, bhikkhave, mayi niha gat, sabbe te dihisampann.
an10.63:1.10 Tesa dihisampannna imesa pacanna idha nih, imesa pacanna idha vihya nihti.
an10.63:1.11 Tatiya. "

an10.65:0.2 7. Yamakavagga
an10.65:0.3 Pahamasukhasutta
an10.65:1.1 Eka samaya yasm sriputto magadhesu viharati nlakagmake.
an10.65:1.2 Atha kho smaakni paribbjako yenyasm sriputto tenupasakami; upasakamitv yasmat sriputtena saddhi sammodi.
an10.65:1.3 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho smaakni paribbjako yasmanta sriputta etadavoca:
an10.65:2.1 Ki nu kho, vuso sriputta, sukha, ki dukkhanti?
an10.65:2.2 Abhinibbatti kho, vuso, dukkh, anabhinibbatti sukh.
an10.65:2.3 Abhinibbattiy, vuso, sati ida dukkha pikakha
an10.65:2.4 sta uha jighacch pips uccro passvo aggisamphasso daasamphasso satthasamphasso tpi mittpi sagamma samgamma rosenti.
an10.65:2.5 Abhinibbattiy, vuso, sati ida dukkha pikakha.
an10.65:2.6 Anabhinibbattiy, vuso, sati ida sukha pikakha
an10.65:2.7 na sta na uha na jighacch na pips na uccro na passvo na aggisamphasso na daasamphasso na satthasamphasso tpi mittpi sagamma samgamma na rosenti.
an10.65:2.8 Anabhinibbattiy, vuso, sati ida sukha pikakhanti.
an10.65:2.9 Pacama. "

an10.66:2.2 Anabhirati kho, vuso, imasmi dhammavinaye dukkh, abhirati sukh.
an10.66:2.3 Anabhiratiy, vuso, sati ida dukkha pikakha

an10.67:0.3 Pahamanaakapnasutta
an10.67:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav kosalesu crika caramno mahat bhikkhusaghena saddhi yena naakapna nma kosalna nigamo tadavasari.
an10.67:1.2 Tatra suda bhagav naakapne viharati palsavane.
an10.67:1.3 Tena kho pana samayena bhagav tadahuposathe bhikkhusaghaparivuto nisinno hoti.
an10.67:1.4 Atha kho bhagav bahudeva ratti bhikkhna dhammiy kathya sandassetv samdapetv samuttejetv sampahasetv tuhbhta tuhbhta bhikkhusagha anuviloketv yasmanta sriputta mantesi:
an10.67:2.1 Vigatathinamiddho kho, sriputta, bhikkhusagho.
an10.67:2.2 Paibhtu ta, sriputta, bhikkhna dhamm kath.
an10.67:2.3 Pihi me gilyati;
an10.67:2.4 tamaha yamissmti.
an10.67:2.5 Eva, bhanteti kho yasm sriputto bhagavato paccassosi.
an10.67:3.1 Atha kho bhagav catuggua saghi papetv dakkhiena passena shaseyya kappesi pde pda accdhya sato sampajno uhnasaa manasi karitv.
an10.67:3.2 Tatra kho yasm sriputto bhikkh mantesi:
an10.67:3.3 vuso bhikkhaveti.
an10.67:3.4 vusoti kho te bhikkh yasmato sriputtassa paccassosu.
an10.67:3.5 yasm sriputto etadavoca:
an10.67:4.1 Yassa kassaci, vuso, saddh natthi kusalesu dhammesu, hir natthi
an10.67:4.2 ottappa natthi
an10.67:4.3 vriya natthi
an10.67:4.4 pa natthi kusalesu dhammesu, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati, hniyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no vuddhi.
an10.67:4.5 Seyyathpi, vuso, kapakkhe candassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati, hyateva vaena hyati maalena hyati bhya hyati rohaparihena;
an10.67:4.6 evameva kho, vuso, yassa kassaci saddh natthi kusalesu dhammesu, hir natthi
an10.67:4.7 ottappa natthi
an10.67:4.8 vriya natthi
an10.67:4.9 pa natthi kusalesu dhammesu, tassa y ratti v divaso v gacchati, hniyeva pikakh kusalesu dhammesu no vuddhi.

an10.69:3.4 rjakatha corakatha mahmattakatha senkatha bhayakatha yuddhakatha annakatha pnakatha vatthakatha sayanakatha mlkatha gandhakatha tikatha ynakatha gmakatha nigamakatha nagarakatha janapadakatha itthikatha srakatha visikhkatha kumbhahnakatha pubbapetakatha nnattakatha lokakkhyika samuddakkhyika itibhavbhavakatha iti vti.

an10.75:0.3 Migaslsutta
an10.75:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav svatthiya viharati jetavane anthapiikassa rme.
an10.75:1.2 Atha kho yasm nando pubbahasamaya nivsetv pattacvaramdya yena migaslya upsikya nivesana tenupasakami; upasakamitv paatte sane nisdi.
an10.75:1.3 Atha kho migasl upsik yenyasm nando tenupasakami; upasakamitv yasmanta nanda abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinn kho migasl upsik yasmanta nanda etadavoca:
an10.75:2.1 Katha katha nmya, bhante nanda, bhagavat dhammo desito aeyyo, yatra hi nma brahmacr ca abrahmacr ca ubho samasamagatik bhavissanti abhisamparya.
an10.75:2.2 Pit me, bhante, puro brahmacr hoti rcr virato methun gmadhamm.
an10.75:2.3 So klakato bhagavat bykato: sakadgm satto tusita kya upapannoti.
an10.75:2.4 Pitmaho me, bhante, isidatto abrahmacr ahosi sadrasantuho.
an10.75:2.5 Sopi klakato bhagavat bykato: sakadgm satto tusita kya upapannoti.
an10.75:3.1 Katha katha nmya, bhante nanda, bhagavat dhammo desito aeyyo, yatra hi nma brahmacr ca abrahmacr ca ubho samasamagatik bhavissanti abhisamparyanti?
an10.75:3.2 Eva kho paneta, bhagini, bhagavat bykatanti.
an10.75:4.1 Atha kho yasm nando migaslya upsikya nivesane piapta gahetv uhysan pakkmi.
an10.75:4.2 Atha kho yasm nando pacchbhatta piaptapaikkanto yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.75:5.1 Idhha, bhante, pubbahasamaya nivsetv pattacvaramdya yena migaslya upsikya nivesana tenupasakami; upasakamitv paatte sane nisdi.
an10.75:5.2 Atha kho, bhante, migasl upsik yenha tenupasakami; upasakamitv ma abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinn kho, bhante, migasl upsik ma etadavoca:
an10.75:6.1 Katha katha nmya, bhante nanda, bhagavat dhammo desito aeyyo, yatra hi nma brahmacr ca abrahmacr ca ubho samasamagatik bhavissanti abhisamparya.
an10.75:6.2 Pit me, bhante, puro brahmacr ahosi rcr virato methun gmadhamm.
an10.75:6.3 So klakato bhagavat bykato sakadgm satto tusita kya upapannoti.
an10.75:6.4 Pitmaho me, bhante, isidatto abrahmacr ahosi sadrasantuho.
an10.75:6.5 Sopi klakato bhagavat bykatosakadgm satto tusita kya upapannoti.
an10.75:7.1 Katha katha nmya, bhante nanda, bhagavat dhammo desito aeyyo, yatra hi nma brahmacr ca abrahmacr ca ubho samasamagatik bhavissanti abhisamparyanti?
an10.75:7.2 Eva vutte, aha, bhante, migasla upsika etadavoca:
an10.75:7.3 eva kho paneta, bhagini, bhagavat bykatanti.
an10.75:8.1 K cnanda, migasl upsik bl abyatt ammak ammakapa, ke ca purisapuggalaparopariye e?
an10.75:9.1 Dasayime, nanda, puggal santo savijjamn lokasmi.
an10.75:9.2 Katame dasa?
an10.75:9.3 Idhnanda, ekacco puggalo dusslo hoti.
an10.75:9.4 Taca cetovimutti pavimutti yathbhta nappajnti, yatthassa ta dussilya aparisesa nirujjhati.
an10.75:9.5 Tassa savanenapi akata hoti, bhusaccenapi akata hoti, dihiypi appaividdha hoti, smyikampi vimutti na labhati.
an10.75:9.6 So kyassa bhed para mara hnya pareti, no visesya;
an10.75:9.7 hnagmyeva hoti, no visesagm.
an10.75:10.1 Idha pannanda, ekacco puggalo dusslo hoti.
an10.75:10.2 Taca cetovimutti pavimutti yathbhta pajnti yatthassa ta dussilya aparisesa nirujjhati.
an10.75:10.3 Tassa savanenapi kata hoti, bhusaccenapi kata hoti, dihiypi paividdha hoti, smyikampi vimutti labhati.
an10.75:10.4 So kyassa bhed para mara visesya pareti, no hnya;
an10.75:10.5 visesagmyeva hoti, no hnagm.
an10.75:11.1 Tatrnanda, pamik pamianti:
an10.75:11.2 imassapi teva dhamm, aparassapi teva dhamm. Kasm nesa eko hno eko patoti?
an10.75:11.3 Tahi tesa, nanda, hoti dgharatta ahitya dukkhya.
an10.75:12.1 Tatrnanda, yvya puggalo dusslo hoti.
an10.75:12.2 Taca cetovimutti pavimutti yathbhta pajnti yatthassa ta dussilya aparisesa nirujjhati.
an10.75:12.3 Tassa savanenapi kata hoti, bhusaccenapi kata hoti, dihiypi paividdha hoti, smyikampi vimutti labhati.
an10.75:12.4 Aya, nanda, puggalo amun purimena puggalena abhikkantataro ca patataro ca.
an10.75:12.5 Ta kissa hetu?
an10.75:12.6 Ima hnanda, puggala dhammasoto nibbahati.
an10.75:12.7 Tadantara ko jneyya, aatra tathgatena.
an10.75:12.8 Tasmtihnanda, m puggalesu pamik ahuvattha,
an10.75:12.9 m puggalesu pama gahittha.
an10.75:12.10 Khaati hnanda, puggalesu pama gahanto.
an10.75:12.11 Aha v, nanda, puggalesu pama gaheyya yo v panassa mdiso.
an10.75:13.1 Idha pannanda, ekacco puggalo slav hoti.
an10.75:13.2 Taca cetovimutti pavimutti yathbhta nappajnti yatthassa ta sla aparisesa nirujjhati.
an10.75:13.3 Tassa savanenapi akata hoti, bhusaccenapi akata hoti, dihiypi appaividdha hoti, smyikampi vimutti na labhati.
an10.75:13.4 So kyassa bhed para mara hnya pareti, no visesya;
an10.75:13.5 hnagmyeva hoti, no visesagm.
an10.75:14.1 Idha pannanda, ekacco puggalo slav hoti.
an10.75:14.2 Taca cetovimutti pavimutti yathbhta pajnti yatthassa ta sla aparisesa nirujjhati.
an10.75:14.3 Tassa savanenapi kata hoti, bhusaccenapi kata hoti, dihiypi paividdha hoti, smyikampi vimutti labhati.
an10.75:14.4 So kyassa bhed para mara visesya pareti, no hnya;
an10.75:14.5 visesagmyeva hoti, no hnagm.

an10.75:26.1 K cnanda, migasl upsik bl abyatt ammak ammakapa, ke ca purisapuggalaparopariye e.
an10.75:26.2 Ime kho, nanda, dasa puggal santo savijjamn lokasmi.
an10.75:27.1 Yathrpena, nanda, slena puro samanngato ahosi tathrpena slena isidatto samanngato abhavissa, nayidha puro isidattassa gatimpi aassa.
an10.75:27.2 Yathrpya cnanda, paya isidatto samanngato ahosi tathrpya paya puro samanngato abhavissa, nayidha isidatto purassa gatimpi aassa.
an10.75:27.3 Iti kho, nanda, ime puggal ubho ekagahnti.
an10.75:27.4 Pacama. "
an10.76:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.76
an10.76:0.2 8. kakhavagga
an10.76:0.3 Tayodhammasutta
an10.76:1.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamm loke na savijjeyyu, na tathgato loke uppajjeyya araha sammsambuddho, na tathgatappavedito dhammavinayo loke dibbeyya.
an10.76:1.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:1.3 Jti ca, jar ca, maraaca
an10.76:1.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamm loke na savijjeyyu, na tathgato loke uppajjeyya araha sammsambuddho, na tathgatappavedito dhammavinayo loke dibbeyya.
an10.76:1.5 Yasm ca kho, bhikkhave, ime tayo dhamm loke savijjanti tasm tathgato loke uppajjati araha sammsambuddho, tasm tathgatappavedito dhammavinayo loke dibbati.
an10.76:2.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo jti pahtu jara pahtu maraa pahtu.
an10.76:2.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:2.3 Rga appahya, dosa appahya, moha appahya
an10.76:2.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo jti pahtu jara pahtu maraa pahtu.
an10.76:3.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo rga pahtu dosa pahtu moha pahtu.
an10.76:3.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:3.3 Sakkyadihi appahya, vicikiccha appahya, slabbataparmsa appahya
an10.76:3.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo rga pahtu dosa pahtu moha pahtu.
an10.76:4.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo sakkyadihi pahtu vicikiccha pahtu slabbataparmsa pahtu.
an10.76:4.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:4.3 Ayonisomanasikra appahya, kummaggasevana appahya, cetaso lnatta appahya
an10.76:4.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo sakkyadihi pahtu vicikiccha pahtu slabbataparmsa pahtu.
an10.76:5.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo ayoniso manasikra pahtu kummaggasevana pahtu cetaso lnatta pahtu.
an10.76:5.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:5.3 Muhassacca appahya, asampajaa appahya, cetaso vikkhepa appahya
an10.76:5.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo ayonisomanasikra pahtu kummaggasevana pahtu cetaso lnatta pahtu.
an10.76:6.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo muhassacca pahtu asampajaa pahtu cetaso vikkhepa pahtu.
an10.76:6.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:6.3 Ariyna adassanakamyata appahya, ariyadhammassa asotukamyata appahya, uprambhacittata appahya
an10.76:6.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo muhassacca pahtu asampajaa pahtu cetaso vikkhepa pahtu.
an10.76:7.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo ariyna adassanakamyata pahtu ariyadhammassa asotukamyata pahtu uprambhacittata pahtu.
an10.76:7.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:7.3 Uddhacca appahya, asavara appahya, dussilya appahya
an10.76:7.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo ariyna adassanakamyata pahtu ariyadhammassa asotukamyata pahtu uprambhacittata pahtu.
an10.76:8.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo uddhacca pahtu asavara pahtu dussilya pahtu.
an10.76:8.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:8.3 Assaddhiya appahya, avadauta appahya, kosajja appahya
an10.76:8.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo uddhacca pahtu asavara pahtu dussilya pahtu.
an10.76:9.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo assaddhiya pahtu avadauta pahtu kosajja pahtu.
an10.76:9.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:9.3 Andariya appahya, dovacassata appahya, ppamittata appahya
an10.76:9.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo assaddhiya pahtu avadauta pahtu kosajja pahtu.
an10.76:10.1 Tayome, bhikkhave, dhamme appahya abhabbo andariya pahtu dovacassata pahtu ppamittata pahtu.
an10.76:10.2 Katame tayo?
an10.76:10.3 Ahirika appahya, anottappa appahya, pamda appahya
an10.76:10.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme appahya abhabbo andariya pahtu dovacassata pahtu ppamittata pahtu.
an10.76:11.1 Ahirikoya, bhikkhave, anottp pamatto hoti.
an10.76:11.2 So pamatto samno abhabbo andariya pahtu dovacassata pahtu ppamittata pahtu.
an10.76:11.3 So ppamitto samno abhabbo assaddhiya pahtu avadauta pahtu kosajja pahtu.
an10.76:11.4 So kusto samno abhabbo uddhacca pahtu asavara pahtu dussilya pahtu.
an10.76:11.5 So dusslo samno abhabbo ariyna adassanakamyata pahtu ariyadhammassa asotukamyata pahtu uprambhacittata pahtu.
an10.76:11.6 So uprambhacitto samno abhabbo muhassacca pahtu asampajaa pahtu cetaso vikkhepa pahtu.
an10.76:11.7 So vikkhittacitto samno abhabbo ayonisomanasikra pahtu kummaggasevana pahtu cetaso lnatta pahtu.
an10.76:11.8 So lnacitto samno abhabbo sakkyadihi pahtu vicikiccha pahtu slabbataparmsa pahtu.
an10.76:11.9 So vicikiccho samno abhabbo rga pahtu dosa pahtu moha pahtu.
an10.76:11.10 So rga appahya dosa appahya moha appahya abhabbo jti pahtu jara pahtu maraa pahtu.

an10.76:20.4 ime kho, bhikkhave, tayo dhamme pahya bhabbo andariya pahtu dovacassata pahtu ppamittata pahtu.
an10.76:21.1 Hirmya, bhikkhave, ottp appamatto hoti.
an10.76:21.2 So appamatto samno bhabbo andariya pahtu dovacassata pahtu ppamittata pahtu.
an10.76:21.3 So kalyamitto samno bhabbo assaddhiya pahtu avadauta pahtu kosajja pahtu.
an10.76:21.4 So raddhavriyo samno bhabbo uddhacca pahtu asavara pahtu dussilya pahtu.
an10.76:21.5 So slav samno bhabbo ariyna adassanakamyata pahtu ariyadhammassa asotukamyata pahtu uprambhacittata pahtu.
an10.76:21.6 So anuprambhacitto samno bhabbo muhassacca pahtu asampajaa pahtu cetaso vikkhepa pahtu.
an10.76:21.7 So avikkhittacitto samno bhabbo ayonisomanasikra pahtu kummaggasevana pahtu cetaso lnatta pahtu.
an10.76:21.8 So alnacitto samno bhabbo sakkyadihi pahtu vicikiccha pahtu slabbataparmsa pahtu.
an10.76:21.9 So avicikiccho samno bhabbo rga pahtu dosa pahtu moha pahtu.
an10.76:21.10 So rga pahya dosa pahya moha pahya bhabbo jti pahtu jara pahtu maraa pahtunti.
an10.76:21.11 Chaha. "

an10.83:0.3 Puiyasutta
an10.83:1.1 Atha kho yasm puiyo yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm puiyo bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.83:1.2 ko nu kho, bhante, hetu ko paccayo yena appekad tathgata dhammadesan paibhti appekad nappaibhtti?
an10.83:2.1 Saddho ca, puiya, bhikkhu hoti, no ca upasakamit; neva tva tathgata dhammadesan paibhti.
an10.83:2.2 Yato ca kho, puiya, bhikkhu saddho ca hoti upasakamit ca, eva tathgata dhammadesan paibhti.
an10.83:3.1 Saddho ca, puiya, bhikkhu hoti upasakamit ca, no ca payirupsit pe
an10.83:3.2 payirupsit ca, no ca paripucchit
an10.83:3.3 paripucchit ca, no ca ohitasoto dhamma suti
an10.83:3.4 ohitasoto ca dhamma suti, no ca sutv dhamma dhreti
an10.83:3.5 sutv ca dhamma dhreti, no ca dhtna dhammna attha upaparikkhati
an10.83:3.6 dhtnaca dhammna attha upaparikkhati no ca atthamaya dhammamaya dhammnudhammappaipanno hoti
an10.83:3.7 atthamaya dhammamaya dhammnudhammappaipanno ca hoti, no ca kalyavco hoti kalyavkkarao poriy vcya samanngato vissahya anelagaya atthassa vipaniy
an10.83:3.8 kalyavco ca hoti kalyavkkarao poriy vcya samanngato vissahya anelagaya atthassa vipaniy, no ca sandassako hoti samdapako samuttejako sampahasako sabrahmacrna, neva tva tathgata dhammadesan paibhti.
an10.83:4.1 Yato ca kho, puiya, bhikkhu saddho ca hoti, upasakamit ca, payirupsit ca, paripucchit ca, ohitasoto ca dhamma suti, sutv ca dhamma dhreti, dhtnaca dhammna attha upaparikkhati, atthamaya dhammamaya dhammnudhammappaipanno ca hoti, kalyavco ca hoti kalyavkkarao poriy vcya samanngato vissahya anelagaya atthassa vipaniy, sandassako ca hoti samdapako samuttejako sampahasako sabrahmacrna
an10.83:4.2 eva tathgata dhammadesan paibhti.
an10.83:4.3 Imehi kho, puiya, dasahi dhammehi samanngat ekantapaibhn tathgata dhammadesan hotti.
an10.83:4.4 Tatiya. "

an10.85:16.17 alika ma, samma, avaca, tucchaka ma, samma, avacaidha khanhti.
an10.85:16.18 So eva vadeyya:
an10.85:16.19 nha ta, samma, alika avaca, tucchaka avaca. Api ca ahameva ummda ppui cetaso vipariyyanti.
an10.85:17.1 Evameva kho, vuso, bhikkhu katth hoti vikatth adhigamesu:
an10.85:17.2 aha pahama jhna sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha dutiya jhna sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha tatiya jhna sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha catuttha jhna sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha ksnacyatana sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha viacyatana sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha kicayatana sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha nevasansayatana sampajjmipi vuhahmipi, aha savedayitanirodha sampajjmipi vuhahmipti.
an10.85:18.1 Tamena tathgato v tathgatasvako v jhy sampattikusalo paracittakusalo paracittapariyyakusalo samanuyujati samanugghati samanubhsati.
an10.85:18.2 So tathgatena v tathgatasvakena v jhyin sampattikusalena paracittakusalena paracittapariyyakusalena samanuyujiyamno samanugghiyamno samanubhsiyamno ira pajjati vicina pajjati anaya pajjati byasana pajjati anayabyasana pajjati.
an10.85:19.1 Tamena tathgato v tathgatasvako v jhy sampattikusalo paracittakusalo paracittapariyyakusalo eva cetas ceto paricca manasi karoti:
an10.85:19.2 ki nu kho ayamyasm katth hoti vikatth adhigamesu
an10.85:19.3 aha pahama jhna sampajjmipi pe
an10.85:19.4 aha savedayitanirodha sampajjmipi vuhahmipti.
an10.85:20.1 Tamena tathgato v tathgatasvako v jhy sampattikusalo paracittapariyyakusalo cetas ceto paricca pajnti:
an10.85:21.1 Dgharatta kho ayamyasm khaakr chiddakr sabalakr kammsakr, na santatakr na santatavutti slesu.
an10.85:21.2 Dusslo kho ayamyasm;
an10.85:21.3 dussilya kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:22.1 Assaddho kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:22.2 assaddhiya kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:23.1 Appassuto kho pana ayamyasm ancro;
an10.85:23.2 appasacca kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:24.1 Dubbaco kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:24.2 dovacassat kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:25.1 Ppamitto kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:25.2 ppamittat kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:26.1 Kusto kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:26.2 kosajja kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:27.1 Muhassati kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:27.2 muhassacca kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:28.1 Kuhako kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:28.2 kohaa kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:29.1 Dubbharo kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:29.2 dubbharat kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:30.1 Duppao kho pana ayamyasm;
an10.85:30.2 duppaat kho pana tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye parihnameta.
an10.85:31.1 So vatvuso, bhikkhu ime dasa dhamme appahya imasmi dhammavinaye vuddhi virhi vepulla pajjissatti neta hna vijjati.
an10.85:31.2 So vatvuso, bhikkhu ime dasa dhamme pahya imasmi dhammavinaye vuddhi virhi vepulla pajjissatti hnameta vijjatti.
an10.85:31.3 Pacama. "

an10.86:2.2 kh jti, vusita brahmacariya, kata karaya, npara itthattyti pajnmti.
an10.86:2.3 Tamena tathgato v tathgatasvako v jhy sampattikusalo paracittakusalo paracittapariyyakusalo samanuyujati samanugghati samanubhsati.
an10.86:2.4 So tathgatena v tathgatasvakena v jhyin sampattikusalena paracittakusalena paracittapariyyakusalena samanuyujiyamno samanugghiyamno samanubhsiyamno ira pajjati vicina pajjati anaya pajjati byasana pajjati anayabyasana pajjati.

an10.86:3.3 kh jti, vusita brahmacariya, kata karaya, npara itthattyti pajnmti.
an10.86:4.1 Tamena tathgato v tathgatasvako v jhy sampattikusalo paracittakusalo paracittapariyyakusalo eva cetas ceto paricca pajnti:

an10.86:5.2 Adhimnena aa bykaroti
an10.86:5.3 kh jti, vusita brahmacariya, kata karaya, npara itthattyti pajnmti.

an10.87:1.1 Tatra kho bhagav klakata bhikkhu rabbha bhikkh mantesi:

an10.87:2.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu adhikaraiko hoti adhikaraasamathassa na vaavd, ayampi dhammo na piyatya na garutya na bhvanya na smaya na ekbhvya savattati.

an10.87:3.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na sikkhkmo hoti sikkhsamdnassa na vaavd, ayampi dhammo na piyatya na garutya na bhvanya na smaya na ekbhvya savattati.

an10.87:4.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu ppiccho hoti icchvinayassa na vaavd, ayampi dhammo na piyatya na garutya na bhvanya na smaya na ekbhvya savattati.

an10.87:7.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu saho hoti sheyyavinayassa na vaavd, ayampi dhammo na piyatya na garutya na bhvanya na smaya na ekbhvya savattati.
an10.87:8.1 Puna capara, bhikkhave, bhikkhu myv hoti, myvinayassa na vaavd.
an10.87:8.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu myv hoti myvinayassa na vaavd, ayampi dhammo na piyatya na garutya na bhvanya na smaya na ekbhvya savattati.

an10.87:10.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na paisallno hoti paisallnassa na vaavd, ayampi dhammo na piyatya na garutya na bhvanya na smaya na ekbhvya savattati.

an10.87:11.2 Yampi, bhikkhave, bhikkhu sabrahmacrna na paisanthrako hoti paisanthrakassa na vaavd, ayampi dhammo na piyatya na garutya na bhvanya na smaya na ekbhvya savattati.
an10.87:12.1 Evarpassa, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno kicpi eva icch uppajjeyya:
an10.87:12.2 aho vata ma sabrahmacr sakkareyyu garu kareyyu mneyyu pjeyyunti, atha kho na sabrahmacr na ceva sakkaronti na garu karonti na mnenti na pjenti.
an10.87:12.3 Ta kissa hetu?
an10.87:12.4 Tathhissa, bhikkhave, vi sabrahmacr te ppake akusale dhamme appahne samanupassanti.
an10.87:13.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, assakhaukassa kicpi eva icch uppajjeyya:
an10.87:13.2 aho vata ma manuss jnyahne hapeyyu, jnyabhojanaca bhojeyyu, jnyaparimajjanaca parimajjeyyunti, atha kho na manuss na ceva jnyahne hapenti na ca jnyabhojana bhojenti na ca jnyaparimajjana parimajjanti.
an10.87:13.3 Ta kissa hetu?
an10.87:13.4 Tathhissa, bhikkhave, vi manuss tni sheyyni keyyni jimheyyni vakeyyni appahnni samanupassanti.
an10.87:13.5 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, evarpassa bhikkhuno kicpi eva icch uppajjeyya:
