an10.88:0.3 Akkosakasutta
an10.88:1.1 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu akkosakaparibhsako ariypavd sabrahmacrna hnameta avakso ya so dasanna byasanna aatara byasana nigaccheyya.
an10.88:1.2 Katamesa dasanna?
an10.88:1.3 Anadhigata ndhigacchati, adhigat parihyati, saddhammassa na vodyanti, saddhammesu v adhimniko hoti anabhirato v brahmacariya carati, aatara v sakiliha patti pajjati, gha v rogtaka phusati, ummda v pputi cittakkhepa, sammho kla karoti, kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjati.
an10.88:1.4 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu akkosakaparibhsako ariypavd sabrahmacrna, hnameta avakso ya so imesa dasanna byasanna aatara byasana nigaccheyyti.
an10.88:1.5 Ahama. "
an10.89:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.89
an10.89:0.2 9. Theravagga
an10.89:0.3 Koklikasutta
an10.89:1.1 Atha kho kokliko bhikkhu yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho kokliko bhikkhu bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.89:1.2 ppicch, bhante, sriputtamoggalln, ppikna icchna vasa gatti.
an10.89:1.3 M heva, koklika, m heva, koklika.
an10.89:1.4 Pasdehi, koklika, sriputtamoggallnesu citta.
an10.89:1.5 Pesal sriputtamoggallnti.
an10.89:2.1 Dutiyampi kho kokliko bhikkhu bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.89:2.2 kicpi me, bhante, bhagav saddhyiko paccayiko, atha kho ppicchva sriputtamoggalln, ppikna icchna vasa gatti.
an10.89:2.3 M heva, koklika, m heva, koklika.
an10.89:2.4 Pasdehi, koklika, sriputtamoggallnesu citta.
an10.89:2.5 Pesal sriputtamoggallnti.
an10.89:3.1 Tatiyampi kho kokliko bhikkhu bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.89:3.2 kicpi me, bhante, bhagav saddhyiko paccayiko, atha kho ppicchva sriputtamoggalln, ppikna icchna vasa gatti.
an10.89:3.3 M heva, koklika, m heva, koklika.
an10.89:3.4 Pasdehi, koklika, sriputtamoggallnesu citta.
an10.89:3.5 Pesal sriputtamoggallnti.
an10.89:4.1 Atha kho kokliko bhikkhu uhysan bhagavanta abhivdetv padakkhia katv pakkmi.
an10.89:4.2 Acirapakkantassa ca koklikassa bhikkhuno ssapamatthi pakhi sabbo kyo phuo ahosi.
an10.89:4.3 Ssapamattiyo hutv muggamattiyo ahesu, muggamattiyo hutv kalyamattiyo ahesu, kalyamattiyo hutv kolahimattiyo ahesu, kolahimattiyo hutv kolamattiyo ahesu, kolamattiyo hutv malakamattiyo ahesu, malakamattiyo hutv tiukamattiyo ahesu, tiukamattiyo hutv, beuvasalukamattiyo ahesu, beuvasalukamattiyo hutv billamattiyo ahesu, billamattiyo hutv pabhijjisu, pubbaca lohitaca paggharisu.
an10.89:4.4 So suda kadalipattesu seti macchova visagilito.
an10.89:5.1 Atha kho tur paccekabrahm yena kokliko bhikkhu tenupasakami; upasakamitv vehse hatv koklika bhikkhu etadavoca:
an10.89:5.2 pasdehi, koklika, sriputtamoggallnesu citta.
an10.89:5.3 Pesal sriputtamoggallnti.
an10.89:5.4 Kosi tva, vusoti?
an10.89:5.5 Aha tur paccekabrahmti.
an10.89:5.6 Nanu tva, vuso, bhagavat angm bykato, atha kicarahi idhgato?
an10.89:5.7 Passa yvaca te ida aparaddhanti.
an10.89:6.1 Atha kho tur paccekabrahm koklika bhikkhu gthhi ajjhabhsi:
an10.89:7.1 Purisassa hi jtassa,
an10.89:7.2 kuhr jyate mukhe;
an10.89:7.3 Yya chindati attna,
an10.89:7.4 blo dubbhsita bhaa.
an10.89:8.1 Yo nindiya pasasati,
an10.89:8.2 Ta v nindati yo pasasiyo;
an10.89:8.3 Vicinti mukhena so kali,
an10.89:8.4 Kalin tena sukha na vindati.
an10.89:9.1 Appamattako aya kali,
an10.89:9.2 Yo akkhesu dhanaparjayo;
an10.89:9.3 Sabbasspi sahpi attan,
an10.89:9.4 Ayameva mahattaro kali;
an10.89:9.5 Yo sugatesu mana padsaye.
an10.89:10.1 Sata sahassna nirabbudna,
an10.89:10.2 Chattisati paca ca abbudni;
an10.89:10.3 Yamariyagarah niraya upeti,
an10.89:10.4 Vca manaca paidhya ppakanti.
an10.89:11.1 Atha kho kokliko bhikkhu teneva bdhena klamaksi.
an10.89:11.2 Klakato ca kokliko bhikkhu paduma niraya upapajjati sriputtamoggallnesu citta ghtetv.
an10.89:12.1 Atha kho brahm sahampati abhikkantya rattiy abhikkantavao kevalakappa jetavana obhsetv yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta ahsi. Ekamanta hito kho brahm sahampati bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.89:12.2 kokliko, bhante, bhikkhu klakato.
an10.89:12.3 Klakato ca, bhante, kokliko bhikkhu paduma niraya upapanno sriputtamoggallnesu citta ghtetvti.
an10.89:12.4 Idamavoca brahm sahampati.
an10.89:12.5 Ida vatv bhagavanta abhivdetv padakkhia katv tatthevantaradhyi.
an10.89:13.1 Atha kho bhagav tass rattiy accayena bhikkh mantesi:
an10.89:13.2 ima, bhikkhave, ratti brahm sahampati abhikkantya rattiy abhikkantavao kevalakappa jetavana obhsetv yenha tenupasakami; upasakamitv ma abhivdetv ekamanta ahsi. Ekamanta hito kho, bhikkhave, brahm sahampati ma etadavoca:
an10.89:13.3 kokliko, bhante, bhikkhu klakato;
an10.89:13.4 klakato ca, bhante, kokliko bhikkhu paduma niraya upapanno sriputtamoggallnesu citta ghtetvti.
an10.89:13.5 Idamavoca, bhikkhave, brahm sahampati.
an10.89:13.6 Ida vatv ma abhivdetv padakkhia katv tatthevantaradhyti.
an10.89:14.1 Eva vutte, aataro bhikkhu bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.89:14.2 kva dgha nu kho, bhante, padume niraye yuppamanti?
an10.89:14.3 Dgha kho, bhikkhu, padume niraye yuppama.
an10.89:14.4 Na ta sukara sakhtu:
an10.89:14.5 ettakni vassnti v ettakni vassasatnti v ettakni vassasahassnti v ettakni vassasatasahassnti vti.
an10.89:15.1 Sakk pana, bhante, upama ktunti?
an10.89:15.2 Sakk, bhikkhti bhagav avoca:
an10.89:15.3 seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsatikhriko kosalako tilavho tato puriso vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena ekameka tila uddhareyya.
an10.89:15.4 Khippatara kho so, bhikkhu, vsatikhriko kosalako tilavho imin upakkamena parikkhaya pariydna gaccheyya, na tveva eko abbudo nirayo.
an10.89:15.5 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati abbud niray; evameko nirabbudo nirayo.
an10.89:15.6 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati nirabbud niray; evameko ababo nirayo.
an10.89:15.7 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati abab niray; evameko aao nirayo.
an10.89:15.8 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati aa niray; evameko ahaho nirayo.
an10.89:15.9 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati ahah niray; evameko kumudo nirayo.
an10.89:15.10 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati kumud niray; evameko sogandhiko nirayo.
an10.89:15.11 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati sogandhik niray; evameko uppalako nirayo.
an10.89:15.12 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati uppalak niray; evameko puarko nirayo.
an10.89:15.13 Seyyathpi, bhikkhu, vsati puark niray; evameko padumo nirayo.
an10.89:15.14 Paduma kho pana, bhikkhu, niraya kokliko bhikkhu upapanno sriputtamoggallnesu citta ghtetvti.
an10.89:15.15 Idamavoca bhagav.
an10.89:15.16 Ida vatvna sugato athpara etadavoca satth:
an10.89:16.1 Purisassa hi jtassa,
an10.89:16.2 kuhr jyate mukhe;
an10.89:16.3 Yya chindati attna,
an10.89:16.4 blo dubbhsita bhaa.
an10.89:17.1 Yo nindiya pasasati,
an10.89:17.2 Ta v nindati yo pasasiyo;
an10.89:17.3 Vicinti mukhena so kali,
an10.89:17.4 Kalin tena sukha na vindati.
an10.89:18.1 Appamattako aya kali,
an10.89:18.2 Yo akkhesu dhanaparjayo;
an10.89:18.3 Sabbasspi sahpi attan,
an10.89:18.4 Ayameva mahattaro kali;
an10.89:18.5 Yo sugatesu mana padsaye.
an10.89:19.1 Sata sahassna nirabbudna,
an10.89:19.2 Chattisati paca ca abbudni;
an10.89:19.3 Yamariyagarah niraya upeti,
an10.89:19.4 Vca manaca paidhya ppakanti.
an10.89:19.5 Navama. "
an10.90:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.90
an10.90:0.2 9. Theravagga
an10.90:0.3 Khsavabalasutta
an10.90:1.1 Atha kho yasm sriputto yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinna kho yasmanta sriputta bhagav etadavoca:
an10.90:1.2 kati nu kho, sriputta, khsavassa bhikkhuno balni, yehi balehi samanngato khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:1.3 kh me savti?
an10.90:2.1 Dasa, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno balni, yehi balehi samanngato khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:2.2 kh me savti.
an10.90:2.3 Katamni dasa?
an10.90:2.4 Idha, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno aniccato sabbe sakhr yathbhta sammappaya sudih honti.
an10.90:2.5 Yampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno aniccato sabbe sakhr yathbhta sammappaya sudih honti, idampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno bala hoti, ya bala gamma khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:2.6 kh me savti.
an10.90:3.1 Puna capara, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno agrakspam km yathbhta sammappaya sudih honti.
an10.90:3.2 Yampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno agrakspam km yathbhta sammappaya sudih honti, idampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno bala hoti, ya bala gamma khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:3.3 kh me savti.
an10.90:4.1 Puna capara, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno vivekaninna citta hoti vivekapoa vivekapabbhra vivekaha nekkhammbhirata byantbhta sabbaso savahniyehi dhammehi.
an10.90:4.2 Yampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno vivekaninna citta hoti vivekapoa vivekapabbhra vivekaha nekkhammbhirata byantbhta sabbaso savahniyehi dhammehi, idampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno bala hoti, ya bala gamma khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:4.3 kh me savti.
an10.90:5.1 Puna capara, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno cattro satipahn bhvit honti subhvit.
an10.90:5.2 Yampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno cattro satipahn bhvit honti subhvit, idampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno bala hoti, ya bala gamma khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:5.3 kh me savti.
an10.90:6.1 Puna capara, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno cattro sammappadhn bhvit honti subhvit pe
an10.90:6.2 cattro iddhipd bhvit honti subhvit pe
an10.90:6.3 pacindriyni
an10.90:6.4 paca balni bhvitni honti subhvitni
an10.90:6.5 satta bojjhag bhvit honti subhvit
an10.90:6.6 ariyo ahagiko maggo bhvito hoti subhvito.
an10.90:6.7 Yampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno ariyo ahagiko maggo bhvito hoti subhvito, idampi, bhante, khsavassa bhikkhuno bala hoti, ya bala gamma khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:6.8 kh me savti.
an10.90:7.1 Imni kho, bhante, dasa khsavassa bhikkhuno balni, yehi balehi samanngato khsavo bhikkhu savna khaya paijnti:
an10.90:7.2 kh me savti.
an10.90:7.3 Dasama.
an10.90:7.4 Theravaggo catuttho.
an10.90:8.0 Tassuddna
an10.90:8.1 Vhannando puiyo,
an10.90:8.2 bykara katthimniko;
an10.90:8.3 Napiyakkosakokli,
an10.90:8.4 khsavabalena cti. "

an10.91:0.2 10. Uplivagga
an10.91:0.3 Kmabhogsutta
an10.91:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav svatthiya viharati jetavane anthapiikassa rme.
an10.91:1.2 Atha kho anthapiiko gahapati yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinna kho anthapiika gahapati bhagav etadavoca:
an10.91:2.1 Dasayime, gahapati, kmabhog santo savijjamn lokasmi.
an10.91:2.2 Katame dasa?
an10.91:2.3 Idha, gahapati, ekacco kmabhog adhammena bhoge pariyesati shasena;
an10.91:2.4 adhammena bhoge pariyesitv shasena na attna sukheti na peti na savibhajati na puni karoti.
an10.91:3.1 Idha pana, gahapati, ekacco kmabhog adhammena bhoge pariyesati shasena;

an10.91:10.3 Te ca bhoge gathito mucchito ajjhosanno andnavadassv anissaraapao paribhujati.
an10.91:11.1 Idha pana, gahapati, ekacco kmabhog dhammena bhoge pariyesati ashasena;
an10.91:11.2 dhammena bhoge pariyesitv ashasena attna sukheti peti savibhajati puni karoti.
an10.91:11.3 Te ca bhoge agathito amucchito anajjhosanno dnavadassv nissaraapao paribhujati.
an10.91:12.1 Tatra, gahapati, yvya kmabhog adhammena bhoge pariyesati shasena, adhammena bhoge pariyesitv shasena na attna sukheti na peti na savibhajati na puni karoti, aya, gahapati, kmabhog thi hnehi grayho.
an10.91:12.2 Adhammena bhoge pariyesati shasenti, imin pahamena hnena grayho.
an10.91:12.3 Na attna sukheti na petti, imin dutiyena hnena grayho.
an10.91:12.4 Na savibhajati na puni karotti, imin tatiyena hnena grayho.
an10.91:12.5 Aya, gahapati, kmabhog imehi thi hnehi grayho.
an10.91:13.1 Tatra, gahapati, yvya kmabhog adhammena bhoge pariyesati shasena, adhammena bhoge pariyesitv shasena attna sukheti peti na savibhajati na puni karoti, aya, gahapati, kmabhog dvhi hnehi grayho ekena hnena psaso.
an10.91:13.2 Adhammena bhoge pariyesati shasenti, imin pahamena hnena grayho.
an10.91:13.3 Attna sukheti petti, imin ekena hnena psaso.
an10.91:13.4 Na savibhajati na puni karotti imin dutiyena hnena grayho.
an10.91:13.5 Aya, gahapati, kmabhog imehi dvhi hnehi grayho imin ekena hnena psaso.

an10.91:22.1 Ime kho, gahapati, dasa kmabhog santo savijjamn lokasmi.
an10.91:22.2 Imesa kho, gahapati, dasanna kmabhogna yvya kmabhog dhammena bhoge pariyesati ashasena, dhammena bhoge pariyesitv ashasena attna sukheti peti savibhajati puni karoti, te ca bhoge agathito amucchito anajjhosanno dnavadassv nissaraapao paribhujati, aya imesa dasanna kmabhogna aggo ca seho ca pmokkho ca uttamo ca pavaro ca.
an10.91:22.3 Seyyathpi, gahapati, gav khra, khramh dadhi, dadhimh navanta, navantamh sappi, sappimh sappimao. Sappimao tattha aggamakkhyati.

an10.99:20.1 So cakkhun rpa disv na nimittaggh hoti nnubyajanaggh.

an10.106:10.2 ye ca micchvimuttipaccay aneke ppak akusal dhamm sambhavanti te cassa nijji honti;
an10.106:10.3 sammvimuttipaccay ca aneke kusal dhamm bhvanpripri gacchanti.
an10.106:11.1 Imni kho, bhikkhave, dasa nijjaravatthnti.
an10.106:11.2 Chaha. "
an10.107:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.107
an10.107:0.2 11. Samaasavagga
an10.107:0.3 Dhovanasutta
an10.107:1.1 Atthi, bhikkhave, dakkhiesu janapadesu dhovana nma.
an10.107:1.2 Tattha hoti annampi pnampi khajjampi bhojjampi leyyampi peyyampi naccampi gtampi vditampi.
an10.107:1.3 Attheta, bhikkhave, dhovana; neta natthti vadmi.
an10.107:1.4 Taca kho eta, bhikkhave, dhovana hna gamma pothujjanika anariya anatthasahita na nibbidya na virgya na nirodhya na upasamya na abhiya na sambodhya na nibbnya savattati.
an10.107:2.1 Ahaca kho, bhikkhave, ariya dhovana desessmi, ya dhovana ekantanibbidya virgya nirodhya upasamya abhiya sambodhya nibbnya savattati, ya dhovana gamma jtidhamm satt jtiy parimuccanti, jardhamm satt jarya parimuccanti, maraadhamm satt maraena parimuccanti, sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupysadhamm satt sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupysehi parimuccanti.
an10.107:2.2 Ta sutha, sdhuka manasi karotha, bhsissmti.
an10.107:2.3 Eva, bhanteti kho te bhikkh bhagavato paccassosu.
an10.107:2.4 Bhagav etadavoca:
an10.107:3.1 Katamaca ta, bhikkhave, ariya dhovana, ya dhovana ekantanibbidya virgya nirodhya upasamya abhiya sambodhya nibbnya savattati, ya dhovana gamma jtidhamm satt jtiy parimuccanti, jardhamm satt jarya parimuccanti, maraadhamm satt maraena parimuccanti, sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupysadhamm satt sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupysehi parimuccanti?
an10.107:4.1 Sammdihikassa, bhikkhave, micchdihi niddhot hoti;
an10.107:4.2 ye ca micchdihipaccay aneke ppak akusal dhamm sambhavanti te cassa niddhot honti;
an10.107:4.3 sammdihipaccay ca aneke kusal dhamm bhvanpripri gacchanti.
an10.107:5.1 Sammsakappassa, bhikkhave, micchsakappo niddhoto hoti pe
an10.107:5.2 sammvcassa, bhikkhave, micchvc niddhot hoti
an10.107:5.3 sammkammantassa, bhikkhave, micchkammanto niddhoto hoti
an10.107:5.4 sammjvassa, bhikkhave, micchjvo niddhoto hoti
an10.107:5.5 sammvymassa, bhikkhave, micchvymo niddhoto hoti
an10.107:5.6 sammsatissa, bhikkhave, micchsati niddhot hoti
an10.107:5.7 sammsamdhissa, bhikkhave, micchsamdhi niddhoto hoti
an10.107:5.8 sammissa, bhikkhave, miccha niddhota hoti pe.
an10.107:6.1 Sammvimuttissa, bhikkhave, micchvimutti niddhot hoti;

an10.107:6.3 sammvimuttipaccay ca aneke kusal dhamm bhvanpripri gacchanti.
an10.107:6.4 Ida kho ta, bhikkhave, ariya dhovana ekantanibbidya virgya nirodhya upasamya abhiya sambodhya nibbnya savattati, ya dhovana gamma jtidhamm satt jtiy parimuccanti, jardhamm satt jarya parimuccanti, maraadhamm satt maraena parimuccanti, sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupysadhamm satt sokaparidevadukkhadomanassupysehi parimuccantti.

an10.115:0.2 12. Paccorohaivagga
an10.115:0.3 Tatiyaadhammasutta
an10.115:1.1 Adhammo ca, bhikkhave, veditabbo dhammo ca;
an10.115:1.2 anattho ca veditabbo attho ca.
an10.115:1.3 Adhammaca viditv dhammaca, anatthaca viditv atthaca yath dhammo yath attho tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.115:1.4 Idamavoca bhagav.
an10.115:1.5 Ida vatvna sugato uhysan vihra pvisi.
an10.115:2.1 Atha kho tesa bhikkhna acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
an10.115:2.2 ida kho no, vuso, bhagav sakhittena uddesa uddisitv vitthrena attha avibhajitv uhysan vihra paviho:
an10.115:2.3 adhammo ca, bhikkhave, veditabbo dhammo ca;
an10.115:2.4 anattho ca veditabbo attho ca.
an10.115:2.5 Adhammaca viditv dhammaca, anatthaca viditv atthaca yath dhammo yath attho tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.115:2.6 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajeyyti?
an10.115:3.1 Atha kho tesa bhikkhna etadahosi:
an10.115:3.2 aya kho yasm nando satthu ceva savaito sambhvito ca vina sabrahmacrna.
an10.115:3.3 Pahoti cyasm nando imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajitu.
an10.115:3.4 Yannna maya yenyasm nando tenupasakameyyma; upasakamitv yasmanta nanda etamattha paipuccheyyma.
an10.115:3.5 Yath no yasm nando bykarissati tath na dhressmti.
an10.115:4.1 Atha kho te bhikkh yenyasm nando tenupasakamisu; upasakamitv yasmat nandena saddhi sammodisu.
an10.115:4.2 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdisu. Ekamanta nisinn kho te bhikkh yasmanta nanda etadavocu:
an10.115:5.1 Ida kho no, vuso nanda, bhagav sakhittena uddesa uddisitv vitthrena attha avibhajitv uhysan vihra paviho:
an10.115:5.2 adhammo ca pe
an10.115:5.3 tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.115:6.1 Tesa no, vuso, amhka acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
an10.115:6.2 ida kho no, vuso, bhagavat sakhittena uddesa uddisitv vitthrena attha avibhajitv uhysan vihra paviho
an10.115:6.3 adhammo ca pe
an10.115:6.4 tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.115:6.5 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajeyyti?
an10.115:7.1 Tesa no, vuso, amhka etadahosi:
an10.115:7.2 aya kho yasm nando satthu ceva savaito sambhvito ca vina sabrahmacrna.
an10.115:7.3 Pahoti cyasm nando imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajitu.
an10.115:7.4 Yannna maya yenyasm nando tenupasakameyyma; upasakamitv yasmanta nanda etamattha paipuccheyyma.
an10.115:7.5 Yath no yasm nando bykarissati tath na dhressmti.
an10.115:7.6 Vibhajatu yasm nandoti.
an10.115:8.1 Seyyathpi, vuso, puriso sratthiko sragaves srapariyesana caramno mahato rukkhassa tihato sravato atikkammeva mla atikkamma khandha skhpalse sra pariyesitabba maeyya;
an10.115:8.2 evasampadamida yasmantna satthari sammukhbhte ta bhagavanta atisitv amhe etamattha paipucchitabba maatha.
an10.115:8.3 So hvuso, bhagav jna jnti passa passati, cakkhubhto abhto dhammabhto brahmabhto vatt pavatt atthassa ninnet amatassa dt dhammassm tathgato.
an10.115:8.4 So ceva panetassa klo ahosi ya tumhe bhagavantayeva upasakamitv etamattha paipuccheyytha.
an10.115:8.5 Yath vo bhagav bykareyya tath na dhreyythti.
an10.115:9.1 Addhvuso nanda, bhagav jna jnti passa passati cakkhubhto abhto dhammabhto brahmabhto vatt pavatt atthassa ninnet amatassa dt dhammassm tathgato.
an10.115:9.2 So ceva panetassa klo ahosi ya maya bhagavantayeva upasakamitv etamattha paipuccheyyma,
an10.115:9.3 yath no bhagav bykareyya tath na dhreyyma.
an10.115:9.4 Api cyasm nando satthu ceva savaito sambhvito ca vina sabrahmacrna.
an10.115:9.5 Pahoti cyasm nando imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajitu.

an10.119:1.1 Tena kho pana samayena jussoi brhmao tadahuposathe ssanhto nava khomayuga nivattho allakusamuhi dya bhagavato avidre ekamanta hito hoti.

an10.119:3.3 Te ta ratti tikkhattu paccuhya pajalik aggi namassanti:
an10.119:3.4 paccorohma bhavanta, paccorohma bhavantanti.
an10.119:3.5 Bahukena ca sappitelanavantena aggi santappenti.
an10.119:3.6 Tass ca rattiy accayena patena khdanyena bhojanyena brhmae santappenti.

an10.120:1.13 micchvymassa kho
an10.120:1.14 micchsatiy kho
an10.120:1.15 micchsamdhissa kho
an10.120:1.16 micchassa kho
an10.120:1.17 micchvimuttiy kho ppako vipko
an10.120:1.18 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.120:1.19 So iti paisakhya micchvimutti pajahati;
an10.120:1.20 micchvimuttiy paccorohati.
an10.120:1.21 Aya vuccati, bhikkhave, ariy paccorohati.
an10.120:1.22 Ahama. "
an10.121:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.121
an10.121:0.2 12. Paccorohaivagga
an10.121:0.3 Pubbagamasutta
an10.121:1.1 Sriyassa, bhikkhave, udayato eta pubbagama eta pubbanimitta, yadidaaruugga.
an10.121:1.2 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, kusalna dhammna eta pubbagama eta pubbanimitta, yadidasammdihi.
an10.121:1.3 Sammdihikassa, bhikkhave, sammsakappo pahoti, sammsakappassa sammvc pahoti, sammvcassa sammkammanto pahoti, sammkammantassa sammjvo pahoti, sammjvassa sammvymo pahoti, sammvymassa sammsati pahoti, sammsatissa sammsamdhi pahoti, sammsamdhissa samma pahoti, sammissa sammvimutti pahotti.
an10.121:1.4 Navama. "
an10.122:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.122

an10.167:0.3 Brhmaapaccorohasutta
an10.167:1.1 Tena kho pana samayena jussoi brhmao tadahuposathe ssanhto nava khomayuga nivattho allakusamuhi dya bhagavato avidre ekamanta hito hoti.
an10.167:2.1 Addas kho bhagav jussoi brhmaa tadahuposathe ssanhta nava khomayuga nivattha allakusamuhi dya ekamanta hita.
an10.167:2.2 Disvna jussoi brhmaa etadavoca:
an10.167:2.3 ki nu tva, brhmaa, tadahuposathe ssanhto nava khomayuga nivattho allakusamuhi dya ekamanta hito?
an10.167:2.4 Ki nvajja brhmaakulassti?
an10.167:2.5 Paccoroha, bho gotama, ajja brhmaakulassti.
an10.167:3.1 Yath katha pana, brhmaa, brhmana paccoroha hotti?
an10.167:3.2 Idha, bho gotama, brhma tadahuposathe ssanht nava khomayuga nivatth allena gomayena pathavi opujitv haritehi kusehi pattharitv antar ca vela antar ca agygra seyya kappenti.
an10.167:3.3 Te ta ratti tikkhattu paccuhya pajalik aggi namassanti:
an10.167:3.4 paccorohma bhavanta, paccorohma bhavantanti.
an10.167:3.5 Bahukena ca sappitelanavantena aggi santappenti.
an10.167:3.6 Tass ca rattiy accayena patena khdanyena bhojanyena brhmae santappenti.
an10.167:3.7 Eva, bho gotama, brhmana paccoroha hotti.
an10.167:4.1 Aath kho, brhmaa, brhmana paccoroha hoti, aath ca pana ariyassa vinaye paccoroha hotti.
an10.167:4.2 Yath katha pana, bho gotama, ariyassa vinaye paccoroha hoti?
an10.167:4.3 Sdhu me bhava gotamo tath dhamma desetu yath ariyassa vinaye paccoroha hotti.
an10.167:5.1 Tena hi, brhmaa, suhi, sdhuka manasi karohi; bhsissmti.
an10.167:5.2 Eva, bhoti kho jussoi brhmao bhagavato paccassosi.
an10.167:5.3 Bhagav etadavoca:
an10.167:6.1 Idha, brhmaa, ariyasvako iti paisacikkhati:
an10.167:6.2 ptiptassa kho ppako vipko dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.167:6.3 So iti paisakhya ptipta pajahati;
an10.167:6.4 ptipt paccorohati.
an10.167:7.1 Adinndnassa kho ppako vipko
an10.167:7.2 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.167:7.3 So iti paisakhya adinndna pajahati;
an10.167:7.4 adinndn paccorohati.
an10.167:8.1 Kmesumicchcrassa kho ppako vipko
an10.167:8.2 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.167:8.3 So iti paisakhya kmesumicchcra pajahati;
an10.167:8.4 kmesumicchcr paccorohati.
an10.167:9.1 Musvdassa kho ppako vipko
an10.167:9.2 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.167:9.3 So iti paisakhya musvda pajahati;
an10.167:9.4 musvd paccorohati.
an10.167:10.1 Pisuya vcya kho ppako vipko
an10.167:10.2 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.167:10.3 So iti paisakhya pisua vca pajahati;
an10.167:10.4 pisuya vcya paccorohati.
an10.167:11.1 Pharusya vcya kho ppako vipko
an10.167:11.2 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.167:11.3 So iti paisakhya pharusa vca pajahati;
an10.167:11.4 pharusya vcya paccorohati.
an10.167:12.1 Samphappalpassa kho ppako vipko
an10.167:12.2 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.
an10.167:12.3 So iti paisakhya samphappalpa pajahati;
an10.167:12.4 samphappalp paccorohati.

an10.167:14.3 So iti paisakhya bypda pajahati;

an10.167:15.1 Micchdihiy kho ppako vipko
an10.167:15.2 dihe ceva dhamme abhisamparyacti.

an10.167:15.4 micchdihiy paccorohati.
an10.167:15.5 Eva kho, brhmaa, ariyassa vinaye paccoroha hotti.
an10.167:16.1 Aath kho, bho gotama, brhmana paccoroha hoti, aath ca pana ariyassa vinaye paccoroha hoti.
an10.167:16.2 Imiss, bho gotama, ariyassa vinaye paccorohaiy brhmana paccoroha kala ngghati soasi.
an10.167:16.3 Abhikkanta, bho gotama pe
an10.167:16.4 upsaka ma bhava gotamo dhretu ajjatagge pupeta saraa gatanti.
an10.167:16.5 Pahama. "

an10.172:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.172
an10.172:0.2 17. Jussoivagga
an10.172:0.3 Dutiyaadhammasutta
an10.172:1.1 Adhammo ca, bhikkhave, veditabbo dhammo ca;
an10.172:1.2 anattho ca veditabbo attho ca.
an10.172:1.3 Adhammaca viditv dhammaca, anatthaca viditv atthaca yath dhammo yath attho tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.172:1.4 Idamavoca bhagav.
an10.172:1.5 Ida vatvna sugato uhysan vihra pvisi.
an10.172:2.1 Atha kho tesa bhikkhna acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
an10.172:2.2 ida kho no, vuso, bhagav sakhittena uddesa uddisitv vitthrena attha avibhajitv uhysan vihra paviho:
an10.172:2.3 adhammo ca, bhikkhave, veditabbo dhammo ca;
an10.172:2.4 anattho ca veditabbo attho ca.
an10.172:2.5 Adhammaca viditv dhammaca, anatthaca viditv atthaca yath dhammo yath attho tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.172:2.6 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajeyyti?
an10.172:3.1 Atha kho tesa bhikkhna etadahosi:
an10.172:3.2 aya kho yasm mahkaccno satthu ceva savaito, sambhvito ca vina sabrahmacrna.
an10.172:3.3 Pahoti cyasm mahkaccno imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajitu.
an10.172:3.4 Yannna maya yenyasm mahkaccno tenupasakameyyma; upasakamitv yasmanta mahkaccna etamattha puccheyyma.
an10.172:3.5 Yath no yasm mahkaccno bykarissati tath na dhressmti.
an10.172:4.1 Atha kho te bhikkh yenyasm mahkaccno tenupasakamisu; upasakamitv yasmat mahkaccnena saddhi sammodisu.
an10.172:4.2 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdisu. Ekamanta nisinn kho te bhikkh yasmanta mahkaccna etadavocu:
an10.172:5.1 Ida kho no, vuso kaccna, bhagav sakhittena uddesa uddisitv vitthrena attha avibhajitv uhysan vihra paviho:
an10.172:5.2 adhammo ca, bhikkhave, veditabbo dhammo ca;
an10.172:5.3 anattho ca veditabbo attho ca.
an10.172:5.4 Adhammaca viditv dhammaca, anatthaca viditv atthaca yath dhammo yath attho tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.172:6.1 Tesa no, vuso, amhka acirapakkantassa bhagavato etadahosi:
an10.172:6.2 ida kho no, vuso, bhagav sakhittena uddesa uddisitv vitthrena attha avibhajitv uhysan vihra paviho
an10.172:6.3 adhammo ca, bhikkhave pe
an10.172:6.4 tath paipajjitabbanti.
an10.172:6.5 Ko nu kho imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajeyyti?
an10.172:7.1 Tesa no, vuso, amhka etadahosi:
an10.172:7.2 aya kho yasm mahkaccno satthu ceva savaito, sambhvito ca vina sabrahmacrna.
an10.172:7.3 Pahoti cyasm mahkaccno imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajitu.
an10.172:7.4 Yannna maya yenyasm mahkaccno tenupasakameyyma; upasakamitv yasmanta mahkaccna etamattha paipuccheyyma.
an10.172:7.5 Yath no yasm mahkaccno bykarissati tath na dhressmti.
an10.172:7.6 Vibhajatu yasm mahkaccnoti.
an10.172:8.1 Seyyathpi, vuso, puriso sratthiko sra gaves srapariyesana caramno mahato rukkhassa tihato sravato atikkammeva mla atikkamma khandha skhpalse sra pariyesitabba maeyya.
an10.172:8.2 Evasampadamida yasmantna satthari sammukhbhte ta bhagavanta atisitv amhe etamattha paipucchitabba maatha.
an10.172:8.3 So hvuso, bhagav jna jnti passa passati cakkhubhto abhto dhammabhto brahmabhto vatt pavatt atthassa ninnet amatassa dt dhammassm tathgato.
an10.172:8.4 So ceva panetassa klo ahosi ya tumhe bhagavantayeva upasakamitv etamattha paipuccheyytha.
an10.172:8.5 Yath vo bhagav bykareyya tath na dhreyythti.
an10.172:9.1 Addh, vuso kaccna, bhagav jna jnti passa passati cakkhubhto abhto dhammabhto brahmabhto vatt pavatt atthassa ninnet amatassa dt dhammassm tathgato.

an10.172:26.2 aya kho yasm mahkaccno satthu ceva savaito, sambhvito ca vina sabrahmacrna.
an10.172:26.3 Pahoti cyasm mahkaccno imassa bhagavat sakhittena uddesassa uddihassa vitthrena attha avibhattassa vitthrena attha vibhajitu.

an10.172:26.5 Yath no yasm mahkaccno bykarissati tath na dhressmti.

an10.172:27.2 Tesa no, bhante, yasmat mahkaccnena imehi akkharehi imehi padehi imehi byajanehi attho suvibhattoti.
an10.172:28.1 Sdhu sdhu, bhikkhave.
an10.172:28.2 Paito, bhikkhave, mahkaccno. Mahpao, bhikkhave, mahkaccno.
an10.172:28.3 Macepi tumhe, bhikkhave, upasakamitv etamattha paipuccheyytha, ahampi ceta evameva bykareyya yath ta mahkaccnena bykata.
an10.172:28.4 Eso ceva tassa attho. Evaca na dhreyythti.
an10.172:28.5 Chaha. "

an10.177:1.1 Atha kho jussoi brhmao yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavat saddhi sammodi.

an10.211:2.1 Adinndy hoti, ya ta parassa paravittpakaraa gmagata v araagata v, ta adinna theyyasakhta dt hoti.
an10.211:3.1 Kmesu micchcr hoti, y t mturakkhit piturakkhit mtpiturakkhit bhturakkhit bhaginirakkhit tirakkhit gottarakkhit dhammarakkhit sasmik saparida antamaso mlguaparikkhittpi, tathrpsu critta pajjit hoti.
an10.211:4.1 Musvd hoti, sabhaggato v parisaggato v timajjhagato v pgamajjhagato v rjakulamajjhagato v abhinto sakkhipuho: ehambho purisa, ya jnsi ta vadehti, so ajna v ha: jnmti, jna v ha: na jnmti, apassa v ha: passmti, passa v ha: na passmti. Iti attahetu v parahetu v misakicikkhahetu v sampajnamus bhsit hoti.
an10.211:5.1 Pisuavco hoti, ito sutv amutra akkht imesa bhedya, amutra v sutv imesa akkht amsa bhedya. Iti samaggna v bhett bhinnna v anuppadt vaggrmo vaggarato vagganand, vaggakarai vca bhsit hoti.
an10.211:6.1 Pharusavco hoti, y s vc aak kakkas parakauk parbhisajjan kodhasmant asamdhisavattanik, tathrpi vca bhsit hoti.
an10.211:7.1 Samphappalp hoti, aklavd abhtavd anatthavd adhammavd avinayavd, anidhnavati vca bhsit hoti aklena anapadesa apariyantavati anatthasahita.
an10.211:8.1 Abhijjhlu hoti, ya ta parassa paravittpakaraa ta abhijjht hoti: aho vata ya parassa ta mama assti.
an10.211:9.1 Bypannacitto hoti, paduhamanasakappo: ime satt haantu v bajjhantu v ucchijjantu v vinassantu v m v ahesunti.

an10.211:11.1 natthi dinna, natthi yiha, natthi huta, natthi sukatadukkana kammna phala vipko, natthi aya loko, natthi paro loko, natthi mt, natthi pit, natthi satt opaptik, natthi loke samaabrhma sammaggat sammpaipann ye imaca loka paraca loka saya abhi sacchikatv pavedentti.

an10.211:16.1 Pisuavca pahya pisuya vcya paivirato hotina ito sutv amutra akkht imesa bhedya, amutra v sutv imesa akkht amsa bhedya. Iti bhinnna v sandht sahitna v anuppadt samaggrmo samaggarato samagganand, samaggakarai vca bhsit hoti.

an10.216:2.2 Kammassak, bhikkhave, satt kammadyd kammayon kammabandh kammapaisara, ya kamma karonti
an10.216:2.3 kalya v ppaka vtassa dyd bhavanti.
an10.216:3.1 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco ptipt hoti luddo lohitapi hatapahate niviho, adaypanno sabbapabhtesu.
an10.216:3.2 So sasappati kyena, sasappati vcya, sasappati manas.
an10.216:3.3 Tassa jimha kyakamma hoti, jimha vackamma, jimha manokamma, jimh gati, jimhupapatti.
an10.216:4.1 Jimhagatikassa kho panha, bhikkhave, jimhupapattikassa dvinna gatna aatara gati vadmi
an10.216:4.2 ye v ekantadukkh niray y v sasappajtik tiracchnayoni.
an10.216:4.3 Katam ca s, bhikkhave, sasappajtik tiracchnayoni?
an10.216:4.4 Ahi vicchik satapad nakul bir msik ulk, ye v panaepi keci tiracchnayonik satt manusse disv sasappanti.
an10.216:4.5 Iti kho, bhikkhave, bht bhtassa upapatti hoti.
an10.216:4.6 Ya karoti tena upapajjati.
an10.216:4.7 Upapannamena phass phusanti.
an10.216:4.8 Evamaha, bhikkhave, kammadyd sattti vadmi.

an10.216:5.2 kmesumicchcr hoti
an10.216:5.3 musvd hoti
an10.216:5.4 pisuavco hoti

an10.216:5.12 So sasappati kyena, sasappati vcya, sasappati manas.
an10.216:5.13 Tassa jimha kyakamma hoti, jimha vackamma, jimha manokamma, jimh gati, jimhupapatti.

an10.216:6.6 ya karoti tena upapajjati.

an10.217:0.2 21. Karajakyavagga
an10.217:0.3 Pahamasacetanikasutta
an10.217:1.1 Nha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv byantbhva vadmi.
an10.217:1.2 Taca kho diheva dhamme upapajje v apare v pariyye.
an10.217:1.3 Na tvevha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv dukkhassantakiriya vadmi.
an10.217:2.1 Tatra, bhikkhave, tividh kyakammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti;
an10.217:2.2 catubbidh vackammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti;
an10.217:2.3 tividh manokammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti.
an10.217:3.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, tividh kyakammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti?
an10.217:3.2 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco ptipt hoti, luddo lohitapi hatapahate niviho adaypanno sabbapabhtesu.
an10.217:4.1 Adinndy hoti, ya ta parassa paravittpakaraa gmagata v araagata v, ta adinna theyyasakhta dt hoti.
an10.217:5.1 Kmesumicchcr hoti, y t mturakkhit pe antamaso mlguaparikkhittpi, tathrpsu critta pajjit hoti.
an10.217:6.1 Eva kho, bhikkhave, tividh kyakammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti.
an10.217:7.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, catubbidh vackammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti?
an10.217:7.2 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco musvd hoti. Sabhaggato v parisaggato v timajjhagato v pgamajjhagato v rjakulamajjhagato v abhinto sakkhipuho
an10.217:7.3 ehambho purisa, ya jnsi ta vadehti, so ajna v ha: jnmti, jna v ha: na jnmti, apassa v ha: passmti, passa v ha: na passmti, iti attahetu v parahetu v misakicikkhahetu v sampajnamus bhsit hoti.
an10.217:8.1 Pisuavco hoti, ito sutv amutra akkht imesa bhedya, amutra v sutv imesa akkht amsa bhedya. Iti samaggna v bhett bhinnna v anuppadt vaggrmo vaggarato vagganand, vaggakarai vca bhsit hoti.
an10.217:9.1 Pharusavco hoti, y s vc aak kakkas parakauk parbhisajjan kodhasmant. Asamdhisavattanik, tathrpi vca bhsit hoti.
an10.217:10.1 Samphappalp hoti, aklavd abhtavd anatthavd adhammavd avinayavd, anidhnavati vca bhsit hoti aklena anapadesa apariyantavati anatthasahita.
an10.217:11.1 Eva kho, bhikkhave, catubbidh vackammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti.
an10.217:12.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, tividh manokammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti?
an10.217:12.2 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco abhijjhlu hoti. Ya ta parassa paravittpakaraa, ta abhijjht hoti: aho vata, ya parassa ta mama assti.
an10.217:13.1 Bypannacitto hoti, paduhamanasakappo: ime satt haantu v bajjhantu v ucchijjantu v vinassantu v m v ahesunti.
an10.217:14.1 Micchdihiko hoti, vipartadassano:
an10.217:14.2 natthi dinna pe ye imaca loka paraca loka saya abhi sacchikatv pavedentti.
an10.217:15.1 Eva kho, bhikkhave, tividh manokammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanik dukkhudray dukkhavipk hoti.
an10.217:16.1 Tividhakyakammantasandosabypattiakusalasacetanikhetu v, bhikkhave, satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjanti; catubbidhavackammantasandosabypattiakusalasacetanikhetu v, bhikkhave, satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjanti; tividhamanokammantasandosabypatti akusalasacetanikhetu v, bhikkhave, satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjanti.
an10.217:17.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, apaako mai uddhakhitto yena yeneva patihti suppatihitayeva patihti;
an10.217:17.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, tividhakyakammantasandosabypattiakusalasacetanikhetu v satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjanti; catubbidhavackammantasandosabypattiakusalasacetanikhetu v satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjanti; tividhamanokammantasandosabypattiakusalasacetanikhetu v satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjantti.
an10.217:18.1 Nha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv byantbhva vadmi,
an10.217:18.2 taca kho diheva dhamme upapajje v apare v pariyye.
an10.217:18.3 Na tvevha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv dukkhassantakiriya vadmi.
an10.217:19.1 Tatra, bhikkhave, tividh kyakammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti;
an10.217:19.2 catubbidh vackammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti;
an10.217:19.3 tividh manokammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti.
an10.217:20.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, tividh kyakammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti?
an10.217:20.2 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco ptipt paivirato hoti nihitadao nihitasattho lajj daypanno, sabbapabhtahitnukamp viharati pe.
an10.217:21.1 Adinndn paivirato hoti, ya ta parassa paravittpakaraa gmagata v araagata v, na ta adinna theyyasakhta dt hoti.
an10.217:22.1 Kmesumicchcra pahya, kmesumicchcr paivirato hoti. Y t mturakkhit pe antamaso mlguaparikkhittpi, tathrpsu na critta pajjit hoti.
an10.217:23.1 Eva kho, bhikkhave, tividh kyakammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti.
an10.217:24.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, catubbidh vackammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti?
an10.217:24.2 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco musvda pahya musvd paivirato hoti. Sabhaggato v parisaggato v timajjhagato v pgamajjhagato v rjakulamajjhagato v abhinto sakkhipuho ehambho purisa, ya jnsi ta vadehti, so ajna v ha: na jnmti, jna v ha: jnmti, apassa v ha: na passmti, passa v ha: passmti, iti attahetu v parahetu v misakicikkhahetu v na sampajnamus bhsit hoti.
an10.217:25.1 Pisua vca pahya, pisuya vcya paivirato hotina ito sutv amutra akkht imesa bhedya, amutra v sutv na imesa akkht amsa bhedya. Iti bhinnna v sandht sahitna v anuppadt samaggrmo samaggarato samagganandi, samaggakarai vca bhsit hoti.
an10.217:26.1 Pharusa vca pahya, pharusya vcya paivirato hoti. Y s vc nel kaasukh pemany hadayagam por bahujanakant bahujanamanp, tathrpi vca bhsit hoti.
an10.217:27.1 Samphappalpa pahya, samphappalp paivirato hoti klavd bhtavd atthavd dhammavd vinayavd, nidhnavati vca bhsit hoti klena spadesa pariyantavati atthasahita.
an10.217:28.1 Eva kho, bhikkhave, catubbidh vackammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti.
an10.217:29.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, tividh manokammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti?
an10.217:29.2 Idha, bhikkhave, ekacco anabhijjhlu hoti. Ya ta parassa paravittpakaraa ta anabhijjht hoti: aho vata, ya parassa ta mamassti.
an10.217:30.1 Abypannacitto hoti appaduhamanasakappo: ime satt aver hontu abypajj angh, sukh attna pariharantti.
an10.217:31.1 Sammdihiko hoti avipartadassano:
an10.217:31.2 atthi dinna, atthi yiha pe ye imaca loka paraca loka saya abhi sacchikatv pavedentti.
an10.217:32.1 Eva kho, bhikkhave, tividh manokammantasampatti kusalasacetanik sukhudray sukhavipk hoti.
an10.217:33.1 Tividhakyakammantasampattikusalasacetanikhetu v, bhikkhave, satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjanti; catubbidhavackammantasampattikusalasacetanikhetu v, bhikkhave, satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjanti; tividhamanokammantasampattikusalasacetanikhetu v, bhikkhave, satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjanti.
an10.217:34.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, apaako mai uddhakhitto yena yeneva patihti suppatihitayeva patihti;
an10.217:34.2 evameva kho, bhikkhave, tividhakyakammantasampattikusalasacetanikhetu v satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjanti; catubbidhavackammantasampattikusalasacetanikhetu v satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjanti; tividhamanokammantasampattikusalasacetanikhetu v satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjanti.
an10.217:34.3 Nha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv byantbhva vadmi.
an10.217:34.4 Taca kho diheva dhamme upapajje v apare v pariyye.
an10.217:34.5 Na tvevha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv dukkhassantakiriya vadmti.
an10.217:34.6 Sattama. "

an10.219:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.219
an10.219:0.2 21. Karajakyavagga
an10.219:0.3 Karajakyasutta
an10.219:1.1 Nha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv byantbhva vadmi,
an10.219:1.2 taca kho diheva dhamme upapajje v apare v pariyye.
an10.219:1.3 Na tvevha, bhikkhave, sacetanikna kammna katna upacitna appaisaveditv dukkhassantakiriya vadmi.
an10.219:2.1 Sa kho so, bhikkhave, ariyasvako eva vigatbhijjho vigatabypdo asammho sampajno paissato mettsahagatena cetas eka disa pharitv viharati tath dutiya tath tatiya tath catuttha. Iti uddhamadho tiriya sabbadhi sabbattatya sabbvanta loka mettsahagatena cetas vipulena mahaggatena appamena averena abypajjena pharitv viharati.
an10.219:3.1 So eva pajnti:
an10.219:3.2 pubbe kho me ida citta paritta ahosi abhvita, etarahi pana me ida citta appama subhvita. Ya kho pana kici pamakata kamma, na ta tatrvasissati na ta tatrvatihatti.
an10.219:4.1 Ta ki maatha, bhikkhave,
an10.219:4.2 daharatagge ce so aya kumro metta cetovimutti bhveyya, api nu kho ppakamma kareyyti?
an10.219:4.3 No heta, bhante.
an10.219:5.1 Akaronta kho pana ppakamma api nu kho dukkha phuseyyti?
an10.219:5.2 No heta, bhante.
an10.219:5.3 Akarontahi, bhante, ppakamma kuto dukkha phusissatti.
an10.219:6.1 Bhvetabb kho panya, bhikkhave, mettcetovimutti itthiy v purisena v.
an10.219:6.2 Itthiy v, bhikkhave, purisassa v nya kyo dya gamanyo.
an10.219:6.3 Cittantaro aya, bhikkhave, macco.
an10.219:6.4 So eva pajnti:
an10.219:6.5 ya kho me ida kici pubbe imin karajakyena ppakamma kata, sabba ta idha vedanya;
an10.219:6.6 na ta anuga bhavissatti.
an10.219:6.7 Eva bhvit kho, bhikkhave, mett cetovimutti angmitya savattati, idha paassa bhikkhuno uttari vimutti appaivijjhato.
an10.219:7.1 Karusahagatena cetas
an10.219:7.2 muditsahagatena cetas
an10.219:7.3 upekkhsahagatena cetas eka disa pharitv viharati tath dutiya tath tatiya tath catuttha.
an10.219:7.4 Iti uddhamadho tiriya sabbadhi sabbattatya sabbvanta loka upekkhsahagatena cetas vipulena mahaggatena appamena averena abypajjena pharitv viharati.
an10.219:8.1 So eva pajnti:
an10.219:8.2 pubbe kho me ida citta paritta ahosi abhvita, etarahi pana me ida citta appama subhvita. Ya kho pana kici pamakata kamma, na ta tatrvasissati na ta tatrvatihatti.
an10.219:9.1 Ta ki maatha, bhikkhave,
an10.219:9.2 daharatagge ce so aya kumro upekkha cetovimutti bhveyya, api nu kho ppakamma kareyyti?
an10.219:9.3 No heta, bhante.
an10.219:10.1 Akaronta kho pana ppakamma api nu kho dukkha phuseyyti?
an10.219:10.2 No heta, bhante.
an10.219:10.3 Akarontahi, bhante, ppakamma kuto dukkha phusissatti.
an10.219:11.1 Bhvetabb kho panya, bhikkhave, upekkh cetovimutti itthiy v purisena v.
an10.219:11.2 Itthiy v, bhikkhave, purisassa v nya kyo dya gamanyo.
an10.219:11.3 Cittantaro aya, bhikkhave, macco.
an10.219:11.4 So eva pajnti:
an10.219:11.5 ya kho me ida kici pubbe imin karajakyena ppakamma kata, sabba ta idha vedanya;
an10.219:11.6 na ta anuga bhavissatti.
an10.219:11.7 Eva bhvit kho, bhikkhave, upekkh cetovimutti angmitya savattati, idha paassa bhikkhuno uttari vimutti appaivijjhatoti.
an10.219:11.8 Navama. "
an10.220:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 10.220
an10.220:0.2 21. Karajakyavagga
an10.220:0.3 Adhammacariysutta
an10.220:1.1 Atha kho aataro brhmao yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavat saddhi sammodi.
an10.220:1.2 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho so brhmao bhagavanta etadavoca:
an10.220:1.3 ko nu kho, bho gotama, hetu ko paccayo yena midhekacce satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjantti?
an10.220:1.4 Adhammacariyvisamacariyhetu kho, brhmaa, evamidhekacce satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjantti.
an10.220:2.1 Ko pana, bho gotama, hetu ko paccayo yena midhekacce satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjantti?
an10.220:2.2 Dhammacariysamacariyhetu kho, brhmaa, evamidhekacce satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjantti.
an10.220:3.1 Na kho aha imassa bhoto gotamassa sakhittena bhsitassa vitthrena attha jnmi.
an10.220:3.2 Sdhu me bhava gotamo tath dhamma desetu yathha imassa bhoto gotamassa sakhittena bhsitassa vitthrena attha jneyyanti.
an10.220:3.3 Tena hi, brhmaa, suhi, sdhuka manasi karohi; bhsissmti.
an10.220:3.4 Eva, bhoti kho so brhmao bhagavato paccassosi.
an10.220:3.5 Bhagav etadavoca:
an10.220:4.1 Tividh kho, brhmaa, kyena adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti;
an10.220:4.2 catubbidh vcya adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti;
an10.220:4.3 tividh manas adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti.
an10.220:5.1 Kathaca, brhmaa, tividh kyena adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti pe
an10.220:5.2 eva kho, brhmaa, tividh kyena adhammacariy visamacariy hoti.
an10.220:6.1 Kathaca, brhmaa, catubbidh vcya adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti pe
an10.220:6.2 eva kho, brhmaa, catubbidh vcya adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti.
an10.220:7.1 Kathaca, brhmaa, tividh manas adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti pe
an10.220:7.2 eva kho, brhmaa, tividh manas adhammacariyvisamacariy hoti.
an10.220:7.3 Eva adhammacariyvisamacariyhetu kho, brhmaa, evamidhekacce satt kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjanti.
an10.220:8.1 Tividh, brhmaa, kyena dhammacariysamacariy hoti;
an10.220:8.2 catubbidh vcya dhammacariysamacariy hoti;
an10.220:8.3 tividh manas dhammacariysamacariy hoti.
an10.220:9.1 Kathaca, brhmaa, tividh kyena dhammacariysamacariy hoti pe
an10.220:9.2 eva kho, brhmaa, tividh kyena dhammacariysamacariy hoti.
an10.220:10.1 Kathaca, brhmaa, catubbidh vcya dhammacariysamacariy hoti pe
an10.220:10.2 eva kho, brhmaa, catubbidh vcya dhammacariysamacariy hoti.
an10.220:11.1 Kathaca, brhmaa, tividh manas dhammacariysamacariy hoti pe
an10.220:11.2 eva kho, brhmaa, tividh manas dhammacariysamacariy hoti.
an10.220:11.3 Eva dhammacariysamacariyhetu kho, brhmaa, evamidhekacce satt kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapajjantti.
an10.220:12.1 Abhikkanta, bho gotama, abhikkanta, bho gotama pe
an10.220:12.2 upsaka ma bhava gotamo dhretu ajjatagge pupeta saraa gatanti.
an10.220:12.3 Dasama.
an10.220:12.4 Karajakyavaggo pahamo. "

an11.1:1.1 Eva me suta
an11.1:1.2 eka samaya bhagav svatthiya viharati jetavane anthapiikassa rme.
an11.1:1.3 Atha kho yasm nando yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando bhagavanta etadavoca:
an11.1:1.4 kimatthiyni, bhante, kusalni slni kimnisasnti?
an11.1:1.5 Avippaisratthni kho, nanda, kusalni slni avippaisrnisasnti.
an11.1:2.1 Avippaisro pana, bhante, kimatthiyo kimnisaso?
an11.1:2.2 Avippaisro kho, nanda, pmojjattho pmojjnisaso.
an11.1:3.1 Pmojja pana, bhante, kimatthiya kimnisasa?
an11.1:3.2 Pmojja kho, nanda, ptattha ptnisasa.
an11.1:4.1 Pti pana, bhante, kimatthiy kimnisas?
an11.1:4.2 Pti kho, nanda, passaddhatth passaddhnisas.
an11.1:5.1 Passaddhi pana, bhante, kimatthiy kimnisas?
an11.1:5.2 Passaddhi kho, nanda, sukhatth sukhnisas.
an11.1:6.1 Sukha pana, bhante, kimatthiya kimnisasa?
an11.1:6.2 Sukha kho, nanda, samdhattha samdhnisasa.
an11.1:7.1 Samdhi pana, bhante, kimatthiyo kimnisaso?
an11.1:7.2 Samdhi kho, nanda, yathbhtaadassanattho yathbhtaadassannisaso.
an11.1:8.1 Yathbhtaadassana pana, bhante, kimatthiya kimnisasa?
an11.1:8.2 Yathbhtaadassana kho, nanda, nibbidattha nibbidnisasa.
an11.1:9.1 Nibbid pana, bhante, kimatthiy kimnisas?
an11.1:9.2 Nibbid kho, nanda, virgatth virgnisas.
an11.1:10.1 Virgo pana, bhante, kimatthiyo kimnisaso?
an11.1:10.2 Virgo kho, nanda, vimuttiadassanattho vimuttiadassannisaso.
an11.1:11.1 Iti kho, nanda, kusalni slni avippaisratthni avippaisrnisasni,
an11.1:11.2 avippaisro pmojjattho pmojjnisaso,
an11.1:11.3 pmojja ptattha ptnisasa,
an11.1:11.4 pti passaddhatth passaddhnisas,
an11.1:11.5 passaddhi sukhatth sukhnisas,
an11.1:11.6 sukha samdhattha samdhnisasa,
an11.1:11.7 samdhi yathbhtaadassanattho yathbhtaadassannisaso,
an11.1:11.8 yathbhtaadassana nibbidattha nibbidnisasa,
an11.1:11.9 nibbid virgatth virgnisas,
an11.1:11.10 virgo vimuttiadassanattho vimuttiadassannisaso.
an11.1:11.11 Iti kho, nanda, kusalni slni anupubbena aggya parentti.
an11.1:11.12 Pahama. "
an11.2:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.2
an11.2:0.2 1. Nissayavagga
an11.2:0.3 Cetankarayasutta
an11.2:1.1 Slavato, bhikkhave, slasampannassa na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:1.2 avippaisro me uppajjatti.
an11.2:1.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya slavato slasampannassa avippaisro uppajjati.
an11.2:2.1 Avippaisrissa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:2.2 pmojja me uppajjatti.
an11.2:2.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya avippaisrissa pmojja uppajjati.
an11.2:3.1 Pamuditassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:3.2 pti me uppajjatti.
an11.2:3.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya pamuditassa pti uppajjati.
an11.2:4.1 Ptimanassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:4.2 kyo me passambhatti.
an11.2:4.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya ptimanassa kyo passambhati.
an11.2:5.1 Passaddhakyassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:5.2 sukha vediymti.
an11.2:5.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya passaddhakyo sukha vediyati.
an11.2:6.1 Sukhino, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:6.2 citta me samdhiyatti.
an11.2:6.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya sukhino citta samdhiyati.
an11.2:7.1 Samhitassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:7.2 yathbhta jnmi passmti.
an11.2:7.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya samhito yathbhta jnti passati.
an11.2:8.1 Yathbhta, bhikkhave, jnato passato na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:8.2 nibbindmti.
an11.2:8.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya yathbhta jna passa nibbindati.
an11.2:9.1 Nibbinnassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:9.2 virajjmti.
an11.2:9.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya nibbinno virajjati.
an11.2:10.1 Virattassa, bhikkhave, na cetanya karaya:
an11.2:10.2 vimuttiadassana sacchikaromti.
an11.2:10.3 Dhammat es, bhikkhave, ya viratto vimuttiadassana sacchikaroti.
an11.2:11.1 Iti kho, bhikkhave, virgo vimuttiadassanattho vimuttiadassannisaso, nibbid virgatth virgnisas, yathbhtaadassana nibbidattha nibbidnisasa, samdhi yathbhtaadassanattho yathbhtaadassannisaso, sukha samdhattha samdhnisasa, passaddhi sukhatth sukhnisas, pti passaddhatth passaddhnisas, pmojja ptattha ptnisasa, avippaisro pmojjattho pmojjnisaso, kusalni slni avippaisratthni avippaisrnisasni.
an11.2:11.2 Iti kho, bhikkhave, dhamm dhamme abhisandenti, dhamm dhamme pariprenti apr pra gamanyti.
an11.2:11.3 Dutiya. "
an11.3:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.3
an11.3:0.2 1. Nissayavagga
an11.3:0.3 Pahamaupanissutta
an11.3:1.1 Dusslassa, bhikkhave, slavipannassa hatpaniso hoti avippaisro.
an11.3:1.2 Avippaisre asati avippaisravipannassa hatpanisa hoti pmojja.
an11.3:1.3 Pmojje asati pmojjavipannassa hatpanis hoti pti.
an11.3:1.4 Ptiy asati ptivipannassa hatpanis hoti passaddhi.
an11.3:1.5 Passaddhiy asati passaddhivipannassa hatpanisa hoti sukha.
an11.3:1.6 Sukhe asati sukhavipannassa hatpaniso hoti sammsamdhi.
an11.3:1.7 Sammsamdhimhi asati sammsamdhivipannassa hatpanisa hoti yathbhtaadassana.
an11.3:1.8 Yathbhtaadassane asati yathbhtaadassanavipannassa hatpanis hoti nibbid.
an11.3:1.9 Nibbidya asati nibbidvipannassa hatpaniso hoti virgo.
an11.3:1.10 Virge asati virgavipannassa hatpanisa hoti vimuttiadassana.
an11.3:2.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, rukkho skhpalsavipanno. Tassa papaikpi na pripri gacchati, tacopi pheggupi sropi na pripri gacchati.
an11.3:2.2 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, dusslassa slavipannassa hatpaniso hoti avippaisro,
an11.3:2.3 avippaisre asati avippaisravipannassa hatpanisa hoti pmojja pe
an11.3:2.4 vimuttiadassana.
an11.3:3.1 Slavato, bhikkhave, slasampannassa upanisasampanno hoti avippaisro,
an11.3:3.2 avippaisre sati avippaisrasampannassa upanisasampanna hoti pmojja,
an11.3:3.3 pmojje sati pmojjasampannassa upanisasampann hoti pti,
an11.3:3.4 ptiy sati ptisampannassa upanisasampann hoti passaddhi,
an11.3:3.5 passaddhiy sati passaddhisampannassa upanisasampanna hoti sukha,
an11.3:3.6 sukhe sati sukhasampannassa upanisasampanno hoti sammsamdhi,
an11.3:3.7 sammsamdhimhi sati sammsamdhisampannassa upanisasampanna hoti yathbhtaadassana,
an11.3:3.8 yathbhtaadassane sati yathbhtaadassanasampannassa upanisasampann hoti nibbid,
an11.3:3.9 nibbidya sati nibbidsampannassa upanisasampanno hoti virgo,
an11.3:3.10 virge sati virgasampannassa upanisasampanna hoti vimuttiadassana.
an11.3:4.1 Seyyathpi, bhikkhave, rukkho skhpalsasampanno. Tassa papaikpi pripri gacchati, tacopi pheggupi sropi pripri gacchati.
an11.3:4.2 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, slavato slasampannassa upanisasampanno hoti avippaisro,
an11.3:4.3 avippaisre sati avippaisrasampannassa upanisasampanna hoti pe
an11.3:4.4 vimuttiadassananti.
an11.3:4.5 Tatiya. "

an11.6:0.3 Byasanasutta
an11.6:1.1 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu akkosako paribhsako ariypavdo sabrahmacrna, hnameta avakso ya so ekdasanna byasanna aatara byasana nigaccheyya.
an11.6:2.1 Katamesa ekdasanna?
an11.6:2.2 Anadhigata ndhigacchati,
an11.6:2.3 adhigat parihyati,
an11.6:2.4 saddhammassa na vodyanti,
an11.6:2.5 saddhammesu v adhimniko hoti,
an11.6:2.6 anabhirato v brahmacariya carati,
an11.6:2.7 aatara v sakiliha patti pajjati,
an11.6:2.8 sikkha v paccakkhya hnyvattati,
an11.6:2.9 gha v rogtaka phusati,
an11.6:2.10 ummda v pputi cittakkhepa v,
an11.6:2.11 sammho kla karoti,
an11.6:2.12 kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapajjati
an11.6:2.13 yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu akkosako paribhsako ariypavdo sabrahmacrna, hnameta avakso ya so imesa ekdasanna byasanna aatara byasana nigaccheyya.
an11.6:3.1 Yo so, bhikkhave, bhikkhu akkosako paribhsako ariypavdo sabrahmacrna, ahnameta anavakso ya so ekdasanna byasanna aatara byasana na nigaccheyya.
an11.6:4.1 Katamesa ekdasanna?

an11.6:4.3 adhigat parihyati,

an11.7:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.7
an11.7:0.2 1. Nissayavagga
an11.7:0.3 Sasutta
an11.7:1.1 Atha kho yasm nando yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando bhagavanta etadavoca:
an11.7:2.1 Siy nu kho, bhante, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an11.7:3.1 Siy, nanda, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.7:4.1 Yath katha pana, bhante, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa, sa ca pana assti.
an11.7:5.1 Idhnanda, bhikkhu evasa hoti:
an11.7:5.2 eta santa eta pata, yadida sabbasakhrasamatho sabbpadhipainissaggo tahkkhayo virgo nirodho nibbnanti.
an11.7:5.3 Eva kho, nanda, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa, sa ca pana assti.
an11.7:6.1 Atha kho yasm nando bhagavato bhsita abhinanditv anumoditv uhysan bhagavanta abhivdetv padakkhia katv yenyasm sriputto tenupasakami; upasakamitv yasmat sriputtena saddhi sammodi.
an11.7:6.2 Sammodanya katha sraya vtisretv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando yasmanta sriputta etadavoca:
an11.7:7.1 Siy nu kho, vuso sriputta, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa, sa pana assti.
an11.7:7.2 Siy, vuso nanda, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa, sa ca pana assti.
an11.7:8.1 Yath katha panvuso sriputta, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa, sa ca pana assti?
an11.7:9.1 Idha, vuso nanda, bhikkhu evasa hoti:
an11.7:9.2 eta santa eta pata, yadida sabbasakhrasamatho sabbpadhipainissaggo tahkkhayo virgo nirodho nibbnanti.
an11.7:9.3 Eva kho, vuso nanda, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi na sa assa, sa ca pana assti.
an11.7:10.1 Acchariya, vuso, abbhuta, vuso.
an11.7:10.2 Yatra hi nma satthu ceva svakassa ca atthena attho byajanena byajana sasandissati samessati na viggayhissati, yadida aggapadasmi.
an11.7:10.3 Idnha, vuso, bhagavanta upasakamitv etamattha apucchi.
an11.7:10.4 Bhagavpi me etehi akkharehi etehi padehi etehi byajanehi etamattha byksi, seyyathpi yasm sriputto.
an11.7:10.5 Acchariya, vuso, abbhuta, vuso.
an11.7:10.6 Yatra hi nma satthu ceva svakassa ca atthena attho byajanena byajana sasandissati samessati na viggayhissati, yadida aggapadasminti.
an11.7:10.7 Sattama. "
an11.8:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.8

an11.8:1.1 Atha kho yasm nando yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho yasm nando bhagavanta etadavoca:
an11.8:2.1 Siy nu kho, bhante, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath na cakkhu manasi kareyya, na rpa manasi kareyya, na sota manasi kareyya, na sadda manasi kareyya, na ghna manasi kareyya, na gandha manasi kareyya, na jivha manasi kareyya, na rasa manasi kareyya, na kya manasi kareyya, na phohabba manasi kareyya, na pathavi manasi kareyya, na pa manasi kareyya, na teja manasi kareyya, na vya manasi kareyya, na ksnacyatana manasi kareyya, na viacyatana manasi kareyya, na kicayatana manasi kareyya, na nevasansayatana manasi kareyya, na idhaloka manasi kareyya, na paraloka manasi kareyya, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tampi na manasi kareyya;
an11.8:2.2 manasi ca pana kareyyti?
an11.8:3.1 Siy, nanda, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath na cakkhu manasi kareyya, na rpa manasi kareyya, na sota manasi kareyya, na sadda manasi kareyya, na ghna manasi kareyya, na gandha manasi kareyya, na jivha manasi kareyya, na rasa manasi kareyya, na kya manasi kareyya, na phohabba manasi kareyya, na pathavi manasi kareyya, na pa manasi kareyya, na teja manasi kareyya, na vya manasi kareyya, na ksnacyatana manasi kareyya, na viacyatana manasi kareyya, na kicayatana manasi kareyya, na nevasansayatana manasi kareyya, na idhaloka manasi kareyya, na paraloka manasi kareyya, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tampi na manasi kareyya;
an11.8:3.2 manasi ca pana kareyyti.
an11.8:4.1 Yath katha pana, bhante, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath na cakkhu manasi kareyya, na rpa manasi kareyya pe
an11.8:4.2 yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tampi na manasi kareyya;
an11.8:4.3 manasi ca pana kareyyti?
an11.8:5.1 Idhnanda, bhikkhu eva manasi karoti:

an11.9:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.9
an11.9:0.2 1. Nissayavagga
an11.9:0.3 Saddhasutta
an11.9:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav ntike viharati gijakvasathe.
an11.9:1.2 Atha kho yasm saddho yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinna kho yasmanta saddha bhagav etadavoca:
an11.9:2.1 jnyajhyita kho, saddha, jhya;
an11.9:2.2 m khaukajhyita.
an11.9:2.3 Kathaca, khaukajhyita hoti?
an11.9:2.4 Assakhauko hi, saddha, doiy baddho yavasa yavasanti jhyati.
an11.9:2.5 Ta kissa hetu?
an11.9:2.6 Na hi, saddha, assakhaukassa doiy baddhassa eva hoti:
an11.9:2.7 ki nu kho ma ajja assadammasrathi kraa kressati, kimassha paikaromti.
an11.9:2.8 So doiy baddho yavasa yavasanti jhyati.
an11.9:2.9 Evameva kho, saddha, idhekacco purisakhauko araagatopi rukkhamlagatopi sugragatopi kmargapariyuhitena cetas viharati kmargaparetena uppannassa ca kmargassa nissaraa yathbhta nappajnti.
an11.9:2.10 So kmargayeva antara katv jhyati pajjhyati nijjhyati avajjhyati,
an11.9:2.11 bypdapariyuhitena cetas viharati
an11.9:2.12 thinamiddhapariyuhitena cetas viharati
an11.9:2.13 uddhaccakukkuccapariyuhitena cetas viharati
an11.9:2.14 vicikicchpariyuhitena cetas viharati vicikicchparetena, uppannya ca vicikicchya nissaraa yathbhta nappajnti.
an11.9:2.15 So vicikicchayeva antara katv jhyati pajjhyati nijjhyati avajjhyati.
an11.9:2.16 So pathavimpi nissya jhyati, pampi nissya jhyati, tejampi nissya jhyati, vyampi nissya jhyati, ksnacyatanampi nissya jhyati, viacyatanampi nissya jhyati, kicayatanampi nissya jhyati, nevasansayatanampi nissya jhyati, idhalokampi nissya jhyati, paralokampi nissya jhyati, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tampi nissya jhyati.
an11.9:2.17 Eva kho, saddha, purisakhaukajhyita hoti.
an11.9:3.1 Kathaca, saddha, jnyajhyita hoti?
an11.9:3.2 Bhadro hi, saddha, assjnyo doiy baddho na yavasa yavasanti jhyati.
an11.9:3.3 Ta kissa hetu?
an11.9:3.4 Bhadrassa hi, saddha, assjnyassa doiy baddhassa eva hoti:
an11.9:3.5 ki nu kho ma ajja assadammasrathi kraa kressati, kimassha paikaromti.
an11.9:3.6 So doiy baddho na yavasa yavasanti jhyati.
an11.9:3.7 Bhadro hi, saddha, assjnyo yath ia yath bandha yath jni yath kali eva patodassa ajjhoharaa samanupassati.
an11.9:3.8 Evameva kho, saddha, bhadro purisjnyo araagatopi rukkhamlagatopi sugragatopi na kmargapariyuhitena cetas viharati na kmargaparetena, uppannassa ca kmargassa nissaraa yathbhta pajnti,
an11.9:3.9 na bypdapariyuhitena cetas viharati
an11.9:3.10 na thinamiddhapariyuhitena cetas viharati
an11.9:3.11 na uddhaccakukkuccapariyuhitena cetas viharati
an11.9:3.12 na vicikicchpariyuhitena cetas viharati na vicikicchparetena, uppannya ca vicikicchya nissaraa yathbhta pajnti.
an11.9:3.13 So neva pathavi nissya jhyati, na pa nissya jhyati, na teja nissya jhyati, na vya nissya jhyati, na ksnacyatana nissya jhyati, na viacyatana nissya jhyati, na kicayatana nissya jhyati, na nevasansayatana nissya jhyati, na idhaloka nissya jhyati, na paraloka nissya jhyati, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tampi nissya na jhyati;
an11.9:3.14 jhyati ca pana.
an11.9:3.15 Eva jhyica pana, saddha, bhadra purisjnya saind dev sabrahmak sapajpatik rakva namassanti:
an11.9:4.1 Namo te purisjaa,
an11.9:4.2 namo te purisuttama;
an11.9:4.3 Yassa te nbhijnma,
an11.9:4.4 yampi nissya jhyasti.
an11.9:5.1 Eva vutte, yasm saddho bhagavanta etadavoca:
an11.9:5.2 katha jhy pana, bhante, bhadro purisjnyo neva pathavi nissya jhyati, na pa nissya jhyati, na teja nissya jhyati, na vya nissya jhyati, na ksnacyatana nissya jhyati, na viacyatana nissya jhyati, na kicayatana nissya jhyati, na nevasansayatana nissya jhyati, na idhaloka nissya jhyati, na paraloka nissya jhyati, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tampi nissya na jhyati;
an11.9:5.3 jhyati ca pana?
an11.9:5.4 Katha jhyica pana, bhante, bhadra purisjnya saind dev sabrahmak sapajpatik rakva namassanti:
an11.9:6.1 Namo te purisjaa,
an11.9:6.2 namo te purisuttama;
an11.9:6.3 Yassa te nbhijnma,
an11.9:6.4 yampi nissya jhyasti.
an11.9:7.1 Idha, saddha, bhadrassa purisjnyassa pathaviya pathavisa vibht hoti, pasmi posa vibht hoti, tejasmi tejosa vibht hoti, vyasmi vyosa vibht hoti, ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa vibht hoti, viacyatane viacyatanasa vibht hoti, kicayatane kicayatanasa vibht hoti, nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa vibht hoti, idhaloke idhalokasa vibht hoti, paraloke paralokasa vibht hoti, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas, tatrpi sa vibht hoti.
an11.9:7.2 Eva jhy kho, saddha, bhadro purisjnyo neva pathavi nissya jhyati pe

an11.9:7.4 jhyati ca pana.
an11.9:7.5 Eva jhyica pana, saddha, bhadra purisjnya saind dev sabrahmak sapajpatik rakva namassanti:

an11.9:8.2 namo te purisuttama;

an11.12:0.3 Dutiyamahnmasutta
an11.12:1.1 Eka samaya bhagav sakkesu viharati kapilavatthusmi nigrodhrme.
an11.12:1.2 Tena kho pana samayena mahnmo sakko giln vuhito hoti aciravuhito gela.
an11.12:1.3 Tena kho pana samayena sambahul bhikkh bhagavato cvarakamma karonti:
an11.12:1.4 nihitacvaro bhagav temsaccayena crika pakkamissatti.
an11.12:2.1 Assosi kho mahnmo sakko:
an11.12:2.2 sambahul kira bhikkh bhagavato cvarakamma karonti:
an11.12:2.3 nihitacvaro bhagav temsaccayena crika pakkamissatti.
an11.12:2.4 Atha kho mahnmo sakko yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho mahnmo sakko bhagavanta etadavoca:
an11.12:2.5 suta meta, bhante:
an11.12:2.6 sambahul kira bhikkh bhagavato cvarakamma karonti
an11.12:2.7 nihitacvaro bhagav temsaccayena crika pakkamissatti.
an11.12:2.8 Tesa no, bhante, nnvihrehi viharata kenassa vihrena vihtabbanti?
an11.12:3.1 Sdhu sdhu, mahnma.
an11.12:3.2 Eta kho, mahnma, tumhka patirpa kulaputtna ya tumhe tathgata upasakamitv puccheyytha:
an11.12:3.3 tesa no, bhante, nnvihrehi viharata kenassa vihrena vihtabbanti?
an11.12:3.4 Saddho kho, mahnma, rdhako hoti, no assaddho;
an11.12:3.5 raddhavriyo rdhako hoti, no kusto;
an11.12:3.6 upahitassati rdhako hoti, no muhassati;
an11.12:3.7 samhito rdhako hoti, no asamhito;
an11.12:3.8 paav rdhako hoti, no duppao.
an11.12:3.9 Imesu kho tva, mahnma, pacasu dhammesu patihya cha dhamme uttari bhveyysi.
an11.12:4.1 Idha tva, mahnma, tathgata anussareyysi:
an11.12:4.2 itipi so bhagav pe satth devamanussna buddho bhagavti.
an11.12:4.3 Yasmi, mahnma, samaye ariyasvako tathgata anussarati, nevassa tasmi samaye rgapariyuhita citta hoti, na dosapariyuhita citta hoti, na mohapariyuhita citta hoti;
an11.12:4.4 ujugatamevassa tasmi samaye citta hoti tathgata rabbha.
an11.12:4.5 Ujugatacitto kho pana, mahnma, ariyasvako labhati atthaveda, labhati dhammaveda, labhati dhammpasahita pmojja.
an11.12:4.6 Pamuditassa pti jyati, ptimanassa kyo passambhati, passaddhakyo sukha vediyati, sukhino citta samdhiyati.
an11.12:4.7 Ima kho tva, mahnma, buddhnussati gacchantopi bhveyysi, hitopi bhveyysi, nisinnopi bhveyysi, saynopi bhveyysi, kammanta adhihahantopi bhveyysi, puttasambdhasayana ajjhvasantopi bhveyysi.
an11.12:5.1 Puna capara tva, mahnma, dhamma anussareyysi pe
an11.12:5.2 sagha anussareyysi pe
an11.12:5.3 attano sla anussareyysi pe
an11.12:5.4 attano cga anussareyysi pe
an11.12:5.5 devat anussareyysi:
an11.12:5.6 santi dev ctumahrjik pe santi dev tatuttari.
an11.12:5.7 Yathrpya saddhya samanngat t devat ito cut tatthpapann, mayhampi tathrp saddh savijjati.
an11.12:5.8 Yathrpena slena
an11.12:5.9 sutena
an11.12:5.10 cgena
an11.12:5.11 paya samanngat t devat ito cut tatthpapann, mayhampi tathrp pa savijjatti.
an11.12:5.12 Yasmi, mahnma, samaye ariyasvako attano ca tsaca devatna saddhaca slaca sutaca cgaca paaca anussarati, nevassa tasmi samaye rgapariyuhita citta hoti, na dosapariyuhita citta hoti, na mohapariyuhita citta hoti;
an11.12:5.13 ujugatamevassa tasmi samaye citta hoti devat rabbha.
an11.12:5.14 Ujugatacitto kho pana, mahnma, ariyasvako labhati atthaveda, labhati dhammaveda, labhati dhammpasahita pmojja.
an11.12:5.15 Pamuditassa pti jyati, ptimanassa kyo passambhati, passaddhakyo sukha vediyati, sukhino citta samdhiyati.
an11.12:5.16 Ima kho tva, mahnma, devatnussati gacchantopi bhveyysi, hitopi bhveyysi, nisinnopi bhveyysi, saynopi bhveyysi, kammanta adhihahantopi bhveyysi, puttasambdhasayana ajjhvasantopi bhveyysti.
an11.12:5.17 Dutiya. "

an11.13:2.5 Tattha kammantaceva adhihahissmi, bhagavantaca lacchmi klena kla dassanyti.

an11.13:3.2 Nandiyopi kho sakko svatthiya vassvsa upagacchi.
an11.13:3.3 Tattha kammantaceva adhihsi, bhagavantaca labhi klena kla dassanya.

an11.13:6.1 Idha tva, nandiya, tathgata anussareyysi:
an11.13:6.2 itipi so bhagav araha sammsambuddho vijjcaraasampanno sugato lokavid anuttaro purisadammasrathi, satth devamanussna buddho bhagavti.
an11.13:6.3 Iti kho te, nandiya, tathgata rabbha ajjhatta sati upahpetabb.
an11.13:7.1 Puna capara tva, nandiya, dhamma anussareyysi:
an11.13:7.2 svkkhto bhagavat dhammo sandihiko akliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccatta veditabbo vihti.
an11.13:7.3 Iti kho te, nandiya, dhamma rabbha ajjhatta sati upahpetabb.
an11.13:8.1 Puna capara tva, nandiya, kalyamitte anussareyysi:
an11.13:8.2 lbh vata me, suladdha vata me,
an11.13:8.3 yassa me kalyamitt anukampak atthakm ovdak anussakti.
an11.13:8.4 Iti kho te, nandiya, kalyamitte rabbha ajjhatta sati upahpetabb.
an11.13:9.1 Puna capara tva, nandiya, attano cga anussareyysi:
an11.13:9.2 lbh vata me, suladdha vata me,
an11.13:9.3 yoha maccheramalapariyuhitya pajya vigatamalamaccherena cetas agra ajjhvasmi muttacgo payatapi vossaggarato ycayogo dnasavibhgaratoti.
an11.13:9.4 Iti kho te, nandiya, cga rabbha ajjhatta sati upahpetabb.
an11.13:10.1 Puna capara tva, nandiya, devat anussareyysi:
an11.13:10.2 y devat atikkammeva kabakrhrabhakkhna devatna sahabyata aatara manomaya kya upapann, t karaya attano na samanupassanti katassa v paticaya.
an11.13:10.3 Seyyathpi, nandiya, bhikkhu asamayavimutto karaya attano na samanupassati katassa v paticaya;
an11.13:10.4 evameva kho, nandiya, y t devat atikkammeva kabakrhrabhakkhna devatna sahabyata aatara manomaya kya upapann, t karaya attano na samanupassanti katassa v paticaya.
an11.13:10.5 Iti kho te, nandiya, devat rabbha ajjhatta sati upahpetabb.
an11.13:11.1 Imehi kho, nandiya, ekdasahi dhammehi samanngato ariyasvako pajahateva ppake akusale dhamme, na updiyati.
an11.13:11.2 Seyyathpi, nandiya, kumbho nikkujjo vamateva udaka, no vanta paccvamati;
an11.13:11.3 seyyathpi v pana, nandiya, sukkhe tiadye aggi mutto ahaeva gacchati, no daha paccudvattati;
an11.13:11.4 evameva kho, nandiya, imehi ekdasahi dhammehi samanngato ariyasvako pajahateva ppake akusale dhamme, na updiyatti.

an11.14:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.14
an11.14:0.2 2. Anussativagga
an11.14:0.3 Subhtisutta
an11.14:1.1 Atha kho yasm subhti saddhena bhikkhun saddhi yena bhagav tenupasakami; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinna kho yasmanta subhti bhagav etadavoca:
an11.14:1.2 ko nmya, subhti, bhikkhti?
an11.14:1.3 Saddho nmya, bhante, bhikkhu, sudattassa upsakassa putto, saddh agrasm anagriya pabbajitoti.
an11.14:2.1 Kacci panya, subhti, saddho bhikkhu sudattassa upsakassa putto saddh agrasm anagriya pabbajito sandissati saddhpadnesti?
an11.14:2.2 Etassa, bhagav, klo; etassa, sugata, klo,
an11.14:2.3 ya bhagav saddhassa saddhpadnni bhseyya.
an11.14:2.4 Idnha jnissmi yadi v aya bhikkhu sandissati saddhpadnesu yadi v noti.
an11.14:3.1 Tena hi, subhti, suhi, sdhuka manasi karohi; bhsissmti.
an11.14:3.2 Eva, bhanteti kho yasm subhti bhagavato paccassosi.
an11.14:3.3 Bhagav etadavoca:
an11.14:4.1 Idha, subhti, bhikkhu slav hoti, ptimokkhasavarasavuto viharati cragocarasampanno aumattesu vajjesu bhayadassv, samdya sikkhati sikkhpadesu.
an11.14:4.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu slav hoti pe samdya sikkhati sikkhpadesu, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:5.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu bahussuto hoti sutadharo sutasannicayo; ye te dhamm dikaly majjhekaly pariyosnakaly sttha sabyajana kevalaparipua parisuddha brahmacariya abhivadanti, tathrpssa dhamm bahussut honti dht vacas paricit manasnupekkhit dihiy suppaividdh.
an11.14:5.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu bahussuto hoti pe dihiy suppaividdh, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:6.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu kalyamitto hoti kalyasahyo kalyasampavako.
an11.14:6.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu kalyamitto hoti kalyasahyo kalyasampavako, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:7.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu suvaco hoti sovacassakaraehi dhammehi samanngato khamo padakkhiaggh anussani.
an11.14:7.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu suvaco hoti sovacassakaraehi dhammehi samanngato khamo padakkhiaggh anussani, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:8.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu yni tni sabrahmacrna uccvacni kikarayni tatra dakkho hoti analaso tatrupyya vmasya samanngato ala ktu ala savidhtu.
an11.14:8.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu yni tni sabrahmacrna uccvacni kikarayni tatra dakkho hoti analaso tatrupyya vmasya samanngato ala ktu ala savidhtu, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:9.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu dhammakmo hoti piyasamudhro abhidhamme abhivinaye urapmojjo.
an11.14:9.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu dhammakmo hoti piyasamudhro abhidhamme abhivinaye urapmojjo, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:10.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu raddhavriyo viharati akusalna dhammna pahnya, kusalna dhammna upasampadya, thmav dahaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu.
an11.14:10.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu raddhavriyo viharati akusalna dhammna pahnya kusalna dhammna upasampadya thmav dahaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:11.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu catunna jhnna bhicetasikna dihadhammasukhavihrna nikmalbh hoti akicchalbh akasiralbh.
an11.14:11.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu catunna jhnna bhicetasikna dihadhammasukhavihrna nikmalbh hoti akicchalbh akasiralbh, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:12.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati,
an11.14:12.2 seyyathidaekampi jti dvepi jtiyo tissopi jtiyo catassopi jtiyo pacapi jtiyo dasapi jtiyo vsampi jtiyo tisampi jtiyo cattrsampi jtiyo pasampi jtiyo jtisatampi jtisahassampi jtisatasahassampi anekepi savaakappe anekepi vivaakappe anekepi savaavivaakappe: amutrsi evanmo evagotto evavao evamhro evasukhadukkhappaisaved evamyupariyanto, so tato cuto amutra udapdi; tatrpsi evanmo evagotto evavao evamhro evasukhadukkhappaisaved evamyupariyanto, so tato cuto idhpapannoti. Iti skra sauddesa anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati.
an11.14:12.3 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati, seyyathidaekampi jti dvepi jtiyo pe iti skra sauddesa anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati. Idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:13.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu dibbena cakkhun visuddhena atikkantamnusakena satte passati cavamne upapajjamne hne pate suvae dubbae, sugate duggate yathkammpage satte pajnti: ime vata bhonto satt kyaduccaritena samanngat vacduccaritena samanngat manoduccaritena samanngat ariyna upavdak micchdihik micchdihikammasamdn, te kyassa bhed para mara apya duggati vinipta niraya upapann. Ime v pana bhonto satt kyasucaritena samanngat vacsucaritena samanngat manosucaritena samanngat ariyna anupavdak sammdihik sammdihikammasamdn, te kyassa bhed para mara sugati sagga loka upapannti. Iti dibbena cakkhun visuddhena atikkantamnusakena satte passati cavamne upapajjamne hne pate suvae dubbae, sugate duggate yathkammpage satte pajnti.
an11.14:13.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu dibbena cakkhun visuddhena pe yathkammpage satte pajnti, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hoti.
an11.14:14.1 Puna capara, subhti, bhikkhu savna khay ansava cetovimutti pavimutti diheva dhamme saya abhi sacchikatv upasampajja viharati.
an11.14:14.2 Yampi, subhti, bhikkhu savna khay pe sacchikatv upasampajja viharati, idampi, subhti, saddhassa saddhpadna hotti.
an11.14:15.1 Eva vutte yasm subhti bhagavanta etadavoca:
an11.14:15.2 ynimni, bhante, bhagavat saddhassa saddhpadnni bhsitni, savijjanti tni imassa bhikkhuno, ayaca bhikkhu etesu sandissati.
an11.14:16.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu slav hoti, ptimokkhasavarasavuto viharati cragocarasampanno aumattesu vajjesu bhayadassv, samdya sikkhati sikkhpadesu.
an11.14:17.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu bahussuto hoti sutadharo sutasannicayo; ye te dhamm dikaly majjhekaly pariyosnakaly sttha sabyajana kevalaparipua parisuddha brahmacariya abhivadanti, tathrpssa dhamm bahussut honti dht vacas paricit manasnupekkhit dihiy suppaividdh.
an11.14:18.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu kalyamitto hoti kalyasahyo kalyasampavako.
an11.14:19.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu suvaco hoti pe anussani.
an11.14:20.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu yni tni sabrahmacrna uccvacni kikarayni tattha dakkho hoti analaso tatrupyya vmasya samanngato ala ktu ala savidhtu.
an11.14:21.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu dhammakmo hoti piyasamudhro abhidhamme abhivinaye urapmojjo.
an11.14:22.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu raddhavriyo viharati pe thmav dahaparakkamo anikkhittadhuro kusalesu dhammesu.
an11.14:23.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu catunna jhnna bhicetasikna dihadhammasukhavihrna nikmalbh hoti akicchalbh akasiralbh.
an11.14:24.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati, seyyathidaekampi jti dvepi jtiyo pe iti skra sauddesa anekavihita pubbenivsa anussarati.
an11.14:25.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu dibbena cakkhun visuddhena atikkantamnusakena pe yathkammpage satte pajnti.
an11.14:26.1 Aya, bhante, bhikkhu savna khay pe sacchikatv upasampajja viharati.
an11.14:26.2 Ynimni, bhante, bhagavat saddhassa saddhpadnni bhsitni, savijjanti tni imassa bhikkhuno, ayaca bhikkhu etesu sandissatti.
an11.14:27.1 Sdhu sdhu, subhti.
an11.14:27.2 Tena hi tva, subhti, imin ca saddhena bhikkhun saddhi vihareyysi.
an11.14:27.3 Yad ca tva, subhti, kakheyysi tathgata dassanya, imin saddhena bhikkhun saddhi upasakameyysi tathgata dassanyti.
an11.14:27.4 Catuttha. "
