an11.15:0.2 2. Anussativagga
an11.15:0.3 Mettsutta
an11.15:1.1 Mettya, bhikkhave, cetovimuttiy sevitya bhvitya bahulkatya ynkatya vatthukatya anuhitya paricitya susamraddhya ekdasnisas pikakh.
an11.15:2.1 Katame ekdasa?
an11.15:2.2 Sukha supati, sukha paibujjhati, na ppaka supina passati, manussna piyo hoti, amanussna piyo hoti, devat rakkhanti, nssa aggi v visa v sattha v kamati, tuvaa citta samdhiyati, mukhavao vippasdati, asammho kla karoti, uttari appaivijjhanto brahmalokpago hoti.
an11.15:2.3 Mettya, bhikkhave, cetovimuttiy sevitya bhvitya bahulkatya ynkatya vatthukatya anuhitya paricitya susamraddhya ime ekdasnisas pikakhti.
an11.15:2.4 Pacama. "
an11.16:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.16
an11.16:0.2 2. Anussativagga
an11.16:0.3 Ahakangarasutta
an11.16:1.1 Eka samaya yasm nando vesliya viharati beluvagmake.
an11.16:1.2 Tena kho pana samayena dasamo gahapati ahakangaro paliputta anuppatto hoti kenacideva karayena.
an11.16:2.1 Atha kho dasamo gahapati ahakangaro yena kukkurmo yena aataro bhikkhu tenupasakami; upasakamitv ta bhikkhu etadavoca:
an11.16:2.2 kaha nu kho, bhante, yasm nando etarahi viharati?
an11.16:2.3 Dassanakm hi maya, bhante, yasmanta nandanti.
an11.16:2.4 Eso, gahapati, yasm nando vesliya viharati beluvagmaketi.
an11.16:3.1 Atha kho dasamo gahapati ahakangaro paliputte ta karaya tretv yena vesl beluvagmako yenyasm nando tenupasakami; upasakamitv yasmanta nanda abhivdetv ekamanta nisdi. Ekamanta nisinno kho dasamo gahapati ahakangaro yasmanta nanda etadavoca:
an11.16:3.2 atthi nu kho, bhante nanda, tena bhagavat jnat passat arahat sammsambuddhena ekadhammo sammadakkhto, yattha bhikkhuno appamattassa tpino pahitattassa viharato avimutta v citta vimuccati, aparikkh v sav parikkhaya gacchanti, ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputti?
an11.16:3.3 Atthi kho, gahapati, tena bhagavat jnat passat arahat sammsambuddhena ekadhammo sammadakkhto, yattha bhikkhuno appamattassa tpino pahitattassa viharato avimutta v citta vimuccati, aparikkh v sav parikkhaya gacchanti, ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputti.
an11.16:4.1 Katamo pana, bhante nanda, tena bhagavat jnat passat arahat sammsambuddhena ekadhammo sammadakkhto, yattha bhikkhuno appamattassa tpino pahitattassa viharato avimutta v citta vimuccati, aparikkh v sav parikkhaya gacchanti, ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputti?
an11.16:4.2 Idha, gahapati, bhikkhu vivicceva kmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakka savicra vivekaja ptisukha pahama jhna upasampajja viharati.
an11.16:4.3 So iti paisacikkhati:
an11.16:4.4 idampi kho pahama jhna abhisakhata abhisacetayita.
an11.16:4.5 Ya kho pana kici abhisakhata abhisacetayita, tadanicca nirodhadhammanti pajnti.
an11.16:4.6 So tattha hito savna khaya pputi;
an11.16:4.7 no ce savna khaya pputi, teneva dhammargena tya dhammanandiy pacanna orambhgiyna sayojanna parikkhay opaptiko hoti tattha parinibby anvattidhammo tasm lok.
an11.16:4.8 Ayampi kho, gahapati, tena bhagavat jnat passat arahat sammsambuddhena ekadhammo sammadakkhto, yattha bhikkhuno appamattassa tpino pahitattassa viharato avimutta v citta vimuccati, aparikkh v sav parikkhaya gacchanti, ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputi.
an11.16:5.1 Puna capara, gahapati, bhikkhu vitakkavicrna vpasam ajjhatta sampasdana cetaso ekodibhva avitakka avicra samdhija ptisukha dutiya jhna pe
an11.16:5.2 tatiya jhna pe
an11.16:5.3 catuttha jhna upasampajja viharati.
an11.16:5.4 So iti paisacikkhati:
an11.16:5.5 idampi kho catuttha jhna abhisakhata abhisacetayita.
an11.16:5.6 Ya kho pana kici abhisakhata abhisacetayita tadanicca nirodhadhammanti pajnti.
an11.16:5.7 So tattha hito savna khaya pputi;
an11.16:5.8 no ce savna khaya pputi, teneva dhammargena tya dhammanandiy pacanna orambhgiyna sayojanna parikkhay opaptiko hoti tattha parinibby anvattidhammo tasm lok.
an11.16:5.9 Ayampi kho, gahapati, tena bhagavat jnat passat arahat sammsambuddhena ekadhammo sammadakkhto, yattha bhikkhuno appamattassa tpino pahitattassa viharato avimutta v citta vimuccati aparikkh v sav parikkhaya gacchanti, ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputi.
an11.16:6.1 Puna capara, gahapati, bhikkhu mettsahagatena cetas eka disa pharitv viharati tath dutiya tath tatiya tath catuttha. Iti uddhamadho tiriya sabbadhi sabbattatya sabbvanta loka mettsahagatena cetas eka disa pharitv viharati vipulena mahaggatena appamena averena abypajjena pharitv viharati.
an11.16:6.2 So iti paisacikkhati:
an11.16:6.3 ayampi kho mett cetovimutti abhisakhat abhisacetayit.
an11.16:6.4 Ya kho pana kici abhisakhata abhisacetayita tadanicca nirodhadhammanti pajnti.
an11.16:6.5 So tattha hito savna khaya pputi;
an11.16:6.6 no ce savna khaya pputi, teneva dhammargena tya dhammanandiy pacanna orambhgiyna sayojanna parikkhay opaptiko hoti tattha parinibby anvattidhammo tasm lok.
an11.16:6.7 Ayampi kho, gahapati, tena bhagavat jnat pe ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputi.
an11.16:7.1 Puna capara, gahapati, bhikkhu karusahagatena cetas pe
an11.16:7.2 muditsahagatena cetas pe
an11.16:7.3 upekkhsahagatena cetas eka disa pharitv viharati tath dutiya tath tatiya tath catuttha.
an11.16:7.4 Iti uddhamadho tiriya sabbadhi sabbattatya sabbvanta loka upekkhsahagatena cetas vipulena mahaggatena appamena averena abypajjena pharitv viharati.
an11.16:7.5 So iti paisacikkhati:
an11.16:7.6 ayampi kho upekkhcetovimutti abhisakhat abhisacetayit.
an11.16:7.7 Ya kho pana kici abhisakhata abhisacetayita tadanicca nirodhadhammanti pajnti.
an11.16:7.8 So tattha hito savna khaya pputi;
an11.16:7.9 no ce savna khaya pputi, teneva dhammargena tya dhammanandiy pacanna orambhgiyna sayojanna parikkhay opaptiko hoti tattha parinibby anvattidhammo tasm lok.
an11.16:7.10 Ayampi kho, gahapati, tena bhagavat jnat pe ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputi.
an11.16:8.1 Puna capara, gahapati, bhikkhu sabbaso rpasana samatikkam paighasana atthagam nnattasana amanasikr ananto ksoti ksnacyatana upasampajja viharati.
an11.16:8.2 So iti paisacikkhati:
an11.16:8.3 ayampi kho ksnacyatanasampatti abhisakhat abhisacetayit.
an11.16:8.4 Ya kho pana kici abhisakhata abhisacetayita tadanicca nirodhadhammanti pajnti.
an11.16:8.5 So tattha hito savna khaya pputi;
an11.16:8.6 no ce savna khaya pputi, teneva dhammargena tya dhammanandiy pacanna orambhgiyna sayojanna parikkhay opaptiko hoti tattha parinibby anvattidhammo tasm lok.
an11.16:8.7 Ayampi kho, gahapati, tena bhagavat jnat pe ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputi.
an11.16:9.1 Puna capara, gahapati, bhikkhu sabbaso ksnacyatana samatikkamma ananta vianti viacyatana upasampajja viharati pe
an11.16:9.2 sabbaso viacyatana samatikkamma natthi kicti kicayatana upasampajja viharati.
an11.16:9.3 So iti paisacikkhati:
an11.16:9.4 ayampi kho kicayatanasampatti abhisakhat abhisacetayit.
an11.16:9.5 Ya kho pana kici abhisakhata abhisacetayita tadanicca nirodhadhammanti pajnti.
an11.16:9.6 So tattha hito savna khaya pputi;
an11.16:9.7 no ce savna khaya pputi, teneva dhammargena tya dhammanandiy pacanna orambhgiyna sayojanna parikkhay opaptiko hoti tattha parinibby anvattidhammo tasm lok.
an11.16:9.8 Ayampi kho, gahapati, tena bhagavat jnat pe ananuppatta v anuttara yogakkhema anupputti.
an11.16:10.1 Eva vutte dasamo gahapati ahakangaro yasmanta nanda etadavoca:
an11.16:10.2 seyyathpi, bhante nanda, puriso eka nidhimukha gavesanto sakideva ekdasa nidhimukhni adhigaccheyya;
an11.16:10.3 evameva kho aha, bhante, eka amatadvra gavesanto sakideva ekdasa amatadvrni alattha sevanya.
an11.16:10.4 Seyyathpi, bhante, purisassa agra ekdasa dvra. So tasmi agre ditte ekamekenapi dvrena sakkueyya attna sotthi ktu;
an11.16:10.5 evameva kho aha, bhante, imesa ekdasanna amatadvrna ekamekenapi amatadvrena sakkuissmi attna sotthi ktu.
an11.16:10.6 Ime hi nma, bhante, aatitthiy cariyassa cariyadhana pariyesissanti.
an11.16:10.7 Ki panha yasmato nandassa pja na karissmti.
an11.16:11.1 Atha kho dasamo gahapati ahakangaro veslikaca paliputtakaca bhikkhusagha sanniptpetv patena khdanyena bhojanyena sahatth santappesi sampavresi.
an11.16:11.2 Ekamekaca bhikkhu pacceka dussayugena acchdesi, yasmantaca nanda ticvarena.
an11.16:11.3 yasmato nandassa pacasata vihra krpesti.
an11.16:11.4 Chaha. "

an11.17:1.1 Ekdasahi, bhikkhave, agehi samanngato goplako abhabbo gogaa pariharitu phti ktu.
an11.17:1.2 Katamehi ekdasahi?
an11.17:1.3 Idha, bhikkhave, goplako na rpa hoti, na lakkhaakusalo hoti, na sika hret hoti, na vaa paicchdet hoti, na dhma katt hoti, na tittha jnti, na pta jnti, na vthi jnti, na gocarakusalo hoti, anavasesadoh ca hoti, ye te usabh gopitaro gopariyak te na atirekapjya pjet hoti.
an11.17:1.4 Imehi kho, bhikkhave, ekdasahi agehi samanngato goplako abhabbo gogaa pariharitu phti ktu.
an11.17:2.1 Evameva kho, bhikkhave, ekdasahi dhammehi samanngato bhikkhu abhabbo imasmi dhammavinaye vuddhi virhi vepulla pajjitu.
an11.17:2.2 Katamehi ekdasahi?
an11.17:2.3 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na rpa hoti, na lakkhaakusalo hoti, na sika hret hoti, na vaa paicchdet hoti, na dhma katt hoti, na tittha jnti, na pta jnti, na vthi jnti, na gocarakusalo hoti, anavasesadoh ca hoti, ye te bhikkh ther ratta cirapabbajit saghapitaro saghapariyak te na atirekapjya pjet hoti.
an11.17:3.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na rpa hoti?
an11.17:3.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu ya kici rpa () cattri mahbhtni, catunnaca mahbhtna updyarpanti yathbhta nappajnti.
an11.17:3.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na rpa hoti.
an11.17:4.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na lakkhaakusalo hoti?
an11.17:4.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kammalakkhao blo, kammalakkhao paitoti yathbhta nappajnti.
an11.17:4.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na lakkhaakusalo hoti.
an11.17:5.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na sika hret hoti?
an11.17:5.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu uppanna kmavitakka adhivseti nappajahati na vinodeti na byantkaroti na anabhva gameti, uppanna bypdavitakka uppanna vihisvitakka
an11.17:5.3 uppannuppanne ppake akusale dhamme adhivseti nappajahati na vinodeti na byantkaroti na anabhva gameti.
an11.17:5.4 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na sika hret hoti.
an11.17:6.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na vaa paicchdet hoti?
an11.17:6.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu cakkhun rpa disv nimittaggh hoti anubyajanaggh;
an11.17:6.3 yatvdhikaraamena cakkhundriya asavuta viharanta abhijjhdomanass ppak akusal dhamm anvssaveyyu, tassa savarya na paipajjati; na rakkhati cakkhundriya, cakkhundriye savara npajjati.
an11.17:6.4 Sotena sadda sutv
an11.17:6.5 ghnena gandha ghyitv
an11.17:6.6 jivhya rasa syitv
an11.17:6.7 kyena phohabba phusitv
an11.17:6.8 manas dhamma viya nimittaggh hoti anubyajanaggh;
an11.17:6.9 yatvdhikaraamena manindriya asavuta viharanta abhijjhdomanass ppak akusal dhamm anvssaveyyu, tassa savarya na paipajjati; na rakkhati manindriya, manindriye savara npajjati.
an11.17:6.10 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na vaa paicchdet hoti.
an11.17:7.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na dhma katt hoti?
an11.17:7.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na yathsuta yathpariyatta dhamma vitthrena paresa deset hoti.
an11.17:7.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na dhma katt hoti.
an11.17:8.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na tittha jnti?
an11.17:8.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu ye te bhikkh bahussut gatgam dhammadhar vinayadhar mtikdhar, te klena kla upasakamitv na paripucchati na paripahati:
an11.17:8.3 ida, bhante, katha, imassa ko atthoti?
an11.17:8.4 Tassa te yasmanto avivaaceva na vivaranti, anuttnkataca na uttnkaronti, anekavihitesu ca kakhhniyesu dhammesu kakha na paivinodenti.
an11.17:8.5 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na tittha jnti.
an11.17:9.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na pta jnti?
an11.17:9.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu tathgatappavedite dhammavinaye desiyamne na labhati atthaveda, na labhati dhammaveda, na labhati dhammpasahita pmojja.
an11.17:9.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na pta jnti.
an11.17:10.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na vthi jnti?
an11.17:10.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu ariya ahagika magga yathbhta nappajnti.
an11.17:10.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na vthi jnti.
an11.17:11.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na gocarakusalo hoti?
an11.17:11.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu cattro satipahne yathbhta nappajnti.
an11.17:11.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu na gocarakusalo hoti.

an11.17:12.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu anavasesadoh hoti.
an11.17:13.1 Kathaca, bhikkhave, bhikkhu ye te bhikkh ther ratta cirapabbajit saghapitaro saghapariyak, te na atirekapjya pjet hoti?
an11.17:13.2 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu ye te bhikkh ther ratta cirapabbajit saghapitaro saghapariyak, tesu na metta kyakamma paccupahpeti vi ceva raho ca, na metta vackamma na metta manokamma paccupahpeti vi ceva raho ca.
an11.17:13.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhu ye te bhikkh ther ratta cirapabbajit saghapitaro saghapariyak, na te atirekapjya pjet hoti.

an11.18:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.18
an11.18:0.2 2. Anussativagga
an11.18:0.3 Pahamasamdhisutta
an11.18:1.1 Atha kho sambahul bhikkh yena bhagav tenupasakamisu; upasakamitv bhagavanta abhivdetv ekamanta nisdisu. Ekamanta nisinn kho te bhikkh bhagavanta etadavocu:
an11.18:2.1 Siy nu kho, bhante, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an11.18:3.1 Siy, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.18:4.1 Yath katha pana, bhante, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an11.18:5.1 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu evasa hoti:
an11.18:5.2 eta santa eta pata, yadida sabbasakhrasamatho sabbpadhipainissaggo tahkkhayo virgo nirodho nibbnanti.
an11.18:5.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.18:5.4 Ahama. "
an11.19:0.1 Aguttara Nikya 11.19
an11.19:0.2 2. Anussativagga
an11.19:0.3 Dutiyasamdhisutta
an11.19:1.1 Tatra kho bhagav bhikkh mantesi:
an11.19:1.2 bhikkhavoti.
an11.19:1.3 Bhadanteti te bhikkh bhagavato paccassosu.
an11.19:1.4 Bhagav etadavoca:
an11.19:2.1 Siy nu kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa pe na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an11.19:2.2 Bhagavamlak no, bhante, dhamm bhagavanettik bhagavapaisara. Sdhu vata, bhante, bhagavantayeva paibhtu etassa bhsitassa attho. Bhagavato sutv bhikkh dhressantti.
an11.19:3.1 Tena hi, bhikkhave, sutha, sdhuka manasi karotha, bhsissmti.
an11.19:3.2 Eva, bhanteti kho te bhikkh bhagavato paccassosu.
an11.19:3.3 Bhagav etadavoca:
an11.19:4.1 Siy, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.19:5.1 Yath katha pana, bhante, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an11.19:6.1 Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu evasa hoti:
an11.19:6.2 eta santa eta pata, yadida sabbasakhrasamatho sabbpadhipainissaggo tahkkhayo virgo nirodho nibbnanti.
an11.19:6.3 Eva kho, bhikkhave, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.19:6.4 Navama. "

an11.20:2.2 Siy, vuso, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.20:3.1 Yath katha pana, vuso sriputta, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an11.20:4.1 Idha, vuso, bhikkhu evasa hoti:
an11.20:4.2 eta santa eta pata, yadida sabbasakhrasamatho sabbpadhipainissaggo tahkkhayo virgo nirodho nibbnanti.
an11.20:4.3 Eva kho, vuso, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.20:4.4 Dasama. "

an11.21:1.1 Tatra kho yasm sriputto bhikkh mantesi:
an11.21:1.2 siy nu kho, vuso, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?
an11.21:2.1 Dratopi kho maya, vuso, gaccheyyma yasmato sriputtassa santike etassa bhsitassa atthamatu.
an11.21:2.2 Sdhu vatyasmantayeva sriputta paibhtu etassa bhsitassa attho.
an11.21:2.3 yasmato sriputtassa sutv bhikkh dhressantti.
an11.21:3.1 Tenahvuso, sutha, sdhuka manasi karotha; bhsissmti.

an11.21:3.3 yasm sriputto etadavoca:
an11.21:4.1 Siy, vuso, bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
an11.21:5.1 Yath katha panvuso, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa pe yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti?

an11.21:6.2 eta santa eta pata, yadida sabbasakhrasamatho sabbpadhipainissaggo tahkkhayo virgo nirodho nibbnanti.
an11.21:6.3 Eva kho, vuso, siy bhikkhuno tathrpo samdhipailbho yath neva pathaviya pathavisa assa, na pasmi posa assa, na tejasmi tejosa assa, na vyasmi vyosa assa, na ksnacyatane ksnacyatanasa assa, na viacyatane viacyatanasa assa, na kicayatane kicayatanasa assa, na nevasansayatane nevasansayatanasa assa, na idhaloke idhalokasa assa, na paraloke paralokasa assa, yampida diha suta muta vita patta pariyesita anuvicarita manas tatrpi na sa assa; sa ca pana assti.
